Ife tidati, “oh iwe Adamu! Ndithudi uyu ndi mdani wako ndiponso mdani wa mkazi wako. Musalole kuti akutulutseni ku Paradiso ndi kukukhazikani m’mavuto.”
Ndithudi muli ndi lonjezo lathu kuti kumeneko inu simudzamva njala kapena kukhala wamaliseche
Ndiponso inu simudzamva ludzu m’menemo kapena kutentha kwa dzuwa
Koma Satana adamunong’oneza nati, “Oh iwe Adamu! Kodi ndingakulangize mtengo wa moyo wosatha ndiponso ufumu wosatha?”
Ndipo onse adadya chipatso cha mumtengo uja kotero udaonekera umaliseche wawo ndipo adayamba kudziveka masamba a m’munda muja. Kotero Adamu adanyoza lamulo la Ambuye wake ndipo adasochera
Ndipo Ambuye wake adamusankha iye ndipo adamukhululukira ndi kumutsogolera kunjira yoyenera
Mulungu adati, “Chokani inu m’menemo, nonse awiri, ndipo inu mudzakhala adani a wina ndi mnzake. Pamene ulangizi wanga udzavumbulutsidwa kwa inu, iye amene adzautsatira sadzasochera kapena kuona mavuto.”
“Koma iye amene safuna kumvera machenjezo anga, ndithudi, adzakhala movutika ndipo tidzamuukitsa ali wakhungu pa tsiku louka kwa akufa.”
Iye adzati, “Ambuye wanga! Bwanji mwandiukitsa wakhungu, pamene ine ndidali wopenya?”
Mulungu adzati, “Chifukwa chakuti pamene chivumbulutso chathu chinadza kwa iwe udachiiwala. Chimodzimodzi tsiku lino nawenso waiwalidwa.”
Mmenemundimmenetimalipiriramunthu oswa malamulo amene sakhulupirira chivumbulutso cha Ambuye wake. Koma chilango cha m’moyo umene uli nkudza ndi choopsa ndiponso chosatha
Kodi iwo saona mibadwo ya anthu imene tidaiononga iwo asanadze? Iwo amayenda pakati pa nyumba zimene iwo anali kukhalamo. Ndithudi mu zimenezi muli zizindikiro kwa anthu a nzeru
Akadakhala kuti Ambuye wako sadalonjeze ndi kukhazikitsa nthawi, chilango chawo chikanadza kale
Motero pirira pa zimene ali kunena ndipo lemekeza ndi kutamanda Ambuye wako dzuwa lisanatuluke ndiponso lisanalowe. Ndipo muyamike Iye nthawi yausiku ndi yausana kuti iwe udzasangalale
Usasirire zinthu zimene tawapatsa anthu chifukwa zimenezi ndi zosangalatsa za m’moyo uno. Ife tingofuna kuwayesa nazo. Koma mphotho ya Ambuye wako ndi yabwino ndipo ndi yosatha
Ndipo lamulira banja lako kupemphera ndipo ukhale wopirira pokwaniritsa mapemphero. Ife sitipempha zinthu kwa iwe koma Ife timakupatsa zofuna zako. Ndipo mapeto abwino ndi a anthu oopa Mulungu
Iwo adati, “Bwanji iye satipatsa ife chizindikiro chochokera kwa Ambuye wake?” Kodi iwo sadapatsidwe zizindikiro zambiri zimene zili m’mabuku a kale a Mulungu
Ngati Ife tikadawaononga iwo ndi chilango tisadawatumizire ichi, iwo akadati, “Ambuye wathu! Inu mukadatitumizira Mtumwi, ndithudi, ife tikadatsatira chivumbulutso chanu tisadanyozedwe ndi kuchititsidwa manyazi.”
Nena, “onse ali kudikira. Nanunso dikirani ndipo inu mudzadziwa kuti ndani amene adatsatira njira yoyenera ndiponso amene ali otsogozedwa.”
Chayandikira kwa anthu chiweruzo cha ntchito yawo ndi pamene iwo abwerera m’mbuyo monyoza
Palibe chenjezo limene limadza kuchokera kwa Ambuye wawo limene iwo amalimvera kupatula pamene iwo ali kusewera
Ndi mitima yotangwanika, iwo amene amachita zoipa amauzana mwamseri kuti, “Kodi uyu si munthu ngati inu? Kodi inu mukutsatira matsenga pamene muli kuona?”
Iye adati: “Ambuye wanga amadziwa chilichonse chimene chimanenedwa kumwamba ndi pa dziko lapansi ndipo Iye amamva zonse ndiponso amadziwa chinthu china chilichonse.”
Koma ena amati, “Ichi si china koma maloto a bodza! Iyayi! Iye walipeka. Iyayi, iye ndi mlakatuli! Ndipo mulekeni atilangize ife chizindikiro china monga momwe Atumwi akale ankachitira.”
Palibe umodzi wa mizinda imene tidaononga imene idakhulupirira iwo asanadze. Kodi iwo adzakhulupirira
Ndipo Ife, iwe usadabwere sitidatumize ena, koma amuna omwe timawapatsa chivumbulutso. Motero afunse anthu ozindikira ngati iwe siudziwa
Ife sitidawapange iwo ndi matupi amene samadya chakudya kapena amuyaya ayi
Ndipo Ife tidakwaniritsa lonjezo lathu kwa iwo, ndipo tidawapulumutsa iwo pamodzi ndi ena amene Ife tidawafuna koma tidaonongeratu anthu onse ochimwa
Ndithudi tavumbulutsa Buku m’mene muli chikumbutso kwa inu. Kodi mulibe nzeru
Kodi ndi mizinda ingati imene tidaononga imene idali yochita zoipa, ndipo m’malo mwawo tidaikamo anthu ena
Ndipo pamene iwo adaona chilango chathu iwo adayesa kuthawa m’mizinda yawo
“Musathawe koma bwererani kumene mumakhala moyo wa chisangalalo ndi ku nyumba zanu kuti mukafunsidwe.”
Iwo anati, “Tsoka kwa ife! Ndithudi tinali kuchita zoipa.”
Koma kulira kwawo sikunathe mpaka pamene Ife tidawaononga ndi kukhala ngati munda umene wakololedwa
Sitidalengemwamasewerakumwambandidzikolapansi ndi zonse zimene zili pakati pake
Ife tikadafuna kuti tisangalale tikadadzipangira tokha, ngati Ife tikadafunadi kutero
Iyayi! Ife timatumiza choonadi kuti chilimbane ndi bodza ndipo chimaliononga. Taonani, ilo latha. Ndipo tsoka kwa inu chifukwa cha zimene mumanena
Zake ndi zonse zimene zili kumwamba ndi pa dziko lapansi. Ndipo onse amene ali pafupi pake sanyozera kumupembedza Iye ndipo satopa ayi
Iwo amamutamanda Iye masana ndi usiku ndipo sachita ulesi
Kodi iwo asankha milungu ya pa dziko lapansi imene imadzutsa anthu akufa
Kukadakhala milungu ina kumeneko yoonjezera pa Mulungu weniweni, ndithudi, konse kukadaonongeka. Alemekezeke Mulungu, Mwini wa Mpando wa Chifumu, mu zimene akumunenera
Iye sangafunsidwe pa ntchito zimene amachita pamene iwo adzafunsidwa
Kodi kapena iwo asankha milungu ina yoonjezera pa Mulungu weniweni? Nena, “Bweretsani umboni wanu”. Ichi ndi chikumbutso cha amene ndili nawo ndiponso iwo amakedzana. Koma ambiri a iwo sadziwa choonadi motero salabadira
Ndipo Ife sitidatumize iwe usadabadwe, Mtumwi wina aliyense amene sitinamuuze kuti, “Kulibe Mulungu wina koma Ine ndekha, kotero ndi pembedzeni Ine.”
Iwo amati, “Mwini chisoni chosatha wabereka mwana wamwamuna.” Iye alemekezedwe! Amenewo si ena ayi koma akapolo ake olemekezeka
Iwo sayankhula pokhapokha Iye atayankhula, ndipo amachita zinthu potsatira malamulo ake
Iye amadziwa zonse zimene zili patsogolo pawo ndiponso zimene zili m’mbuyo mwawo ndipo iwo sangalankhulire wina aliyense chipulumutso kupatula amene Iye wamukonda ndipo iwo amanjenjemera chifukwa cha mantha pomuona Iye
Ndipo ngati wina wa iwo atanena kuti, “Ndithudi ine ndine mulungu kuonjezera pa Iye.” Oteroyo adzalangidwa ndi moto wa ku Gahena. Mmenemo ndi mmene timalipirira anthu olakwa
Kodi anthu osakhulupirira sadziwa kuti kumwamba ndi dziko lapansi chidali chinthu chimodzi chogwirana chimene tidachisiyanitsa? Ndipo tidapanga, chilichonse chamoyo, kuchokera ku madzi. Kodi iwo sangakhulupirire
Ndipo Ife tidakhazikitsa mapiri pa dziko lapansi molimba kuti asagwedezeke pamodzi ndi iwo ndipo tidakhazikitsa misewu pa miyala kuti mwina atsogozedwe
Ndipo tidapanga kumwamba denga losungika bwino limene silingagwe. Komabe iwo amakana zizindikiro zake
Iye ndiye amene adalenga usiku ndi usana, dzuwa ndi mwezi ndi china chilichonse chimene chimayenda mlengalenga
Palibe munthu, pambuyo pako amene tidamulenga kuti sadzafa. Ngati iweyo udzafa, kodi iwo adzakhala ndi moyo mpaka kalekale
Chilichonse cholengedwa chidzalawa imfa ndipo Ife tidzakuyesani ndi zinthu zoipa ndi zabwino ndipo ndi kwa Ife kumene nonse mudzabwerera
Pamene anthu osakhulupirira amakuona iwe, sakuganizira zabwino koma chipongwe ndipo amati, “Kodi uyu ndiye munthu amene amayankhula zoipa za milungu yanu?” Pamene iwo amakana zonse zokhudza Mwini chisoni chosatha
Munthu adalengedwa kukhala opupuluma pochita zinthu. Ine ndidzakusonyezani zizindikiro zanga. Motero musandifulumizitse
Iwo amati, “Kodi lonjezo limeneli lidzakwaniritsidwa liti ngati zimene uli kunena ndi zoona?”
Akadakhala kuti anthu osakhulupirira akudziwa tsiku limene iwo sadzakhala ndi mphamvu zophimba nkhope kapena misana yawo kudziteteza ku moto ndipo iwo sangathandizike
Iyayi. Ilo lidzadza kwa iwo mwadzidzidzi ndipo adzadodoma ndi kusokonezeka ndipo iwo sadzatha kulibweza ndiponso sadzapatsidwa nthawi yopuma
Ndithudi Atumwi ena, adachitidwa chipongwe kale, koma anthu a chipongwe adafafanizidwa ndi chilango chimene iwo adachichitira chipongwe
Nena, “Kodi ndani adzakutetezani inu nthawi ya usiku ndi nthawi ya masana ku mkwiyo wa Mwini chisoni?” Komabe iwo salabadira zokumbukira Ambuye wawo
Kapena iwo ali ndi milungu ina yoti ingawateteze kwa Ife? Iyo siingathe kudziteteza yokha; ndiponso iwo sangatetezedwe kuchilango chathu
Koma Ife tidapereka zokoma za m’moyo uno kwa anthuwa pamodzi ndi makolo awo mpaka pamene nthawi idawatalikira iwo. Kodi iwo saona kuti Ife timachepetsa dziko lawo kuchokera m’malire mwake? Kodi iwo ndiwo adzapambane
Nena, “Ine ndili kukuchenjezani ndi chivumbulutso, koma agonthi sadzamva kuitana pamene achenjezedwa
Koma ngati katsoka kakang’ono kochokera kwa Ambuye wako kagwa pa iwo, ndithudi, iwo adzalira, “Tsoka kwa ife; ndithudi tidali anthu ochita zoipa.”
Ndipo Ife tidzakhazikitsa miyeso yoyenera pa tsiku la kuuka kwa akufa ndipo aliyense sadzaponderezedwa pa china chilichonse. Ngakhale patakhala ntchito zazing’ono zolingana ngati kanthangala kakang’ono tidzazitulutsa kuti ziyesedwe. Ndipo Ife ndife okwana kuwerengera ntchito zonse
Ndithudi Ife tidamupatsa Mose ndi Aroni muyeso ndi muuni wowala ndi chikumbutso kwa anthu angwiro
Iwo amene amaopa Ambuye kuchokera m’maganizo a pansi penipeni pa mtima ndipo amaopa tsiku louka kwa akufa
Ndipo ichi ndi chivumbulutso chodalitsika chimene tatumiza. Kodi mudzachikana
Ndithudi Ife tidamupatsa kale chilangizo Abrahamu ndipo tinali kumudziwa bwino
Pamene Iye adawauza abambo ake ndiponso anthu ake kuti, “Kodi mafano amene muli kuwapembedzawa ndi chiyani?”
Iwo adati, “Ife tidapeza makolo athu ali kuwapembedza.”
Iye adati, “Ndithudi inu ndiponso makolo anu mwakhala muli kuchimwa kwambiri.”
Iwo adati, “Kodi ndi zoona zimene wadza nazo kwa ife kapena ndi nthabwala chabe?”
Iye adati, “Iyayi. Ambuye wanu ndi amene adalenga kumwamba ndi dziko lapansi ndipo muzimenezo ine ndichitira umboni.”
“Ndilumbira pali Mulungu kuti ine ndidzachita chiwembu pa mafano anu inu mukangochoka.”
Motero iye adaziphwanya zonse kukhala tizidutswa kupatula fano lalikulu kuti akhoza kudzalifunsa
Iwo adati: “Kodi ndani amene wachita izi kwa milungu yathu? Ndithudi iye ali oipitsitsa.”
Iwo adati, “Ife tinamva mnyamata wotchedwa Abrahamu akunena za milunguyo.”
Iwo adati, “Mubweretseni pamaso pa anthu onse kuti achitire umboni.”
Iwo adati, “Kodi iwe ndi amene wachita izi ku milungu yathu? Oh Abrahamu!”
Iye adati, “Iyayi. Ndi uyu, wamkulu kuposa zonse amene waziphwanya. Afunseni, ngati angayankhule”
Pamenepo iwo adayang’anizana okha nati, “Ndithudi inu ndinu anthu ochimwa kwambiri.”
Ndipo adayang’anizananso nati, “Ndithudi iwe uli kudziwa kuti milungu iyi siiyankhula.”
Abrahamu adati, “Kodi inu mumapembedza mowonjezera pa Mulungu zinthu zimene sizingathe kukuthandizani chilichonse kapena kukuonongani?”
“Tsoka likhale pa inu ndi pa mafano anu amene mumapembedza kuonjezera pa Mulungu! Kodi mulibe nzeru?”
Onse adati, “Mutentheni kuti muteteze milungu yanu ngati mufuna kuchita china chilichonse.”
Ife tidati, “Iwe moto khala wozizira ndi wamtendere kwa Abrahamu.”
Ndipo iwo adafuna kumuononga Iye koma Ife tidawapanga iwo kukhala olephera
Koma Ife tidamupulumutsa iye pamodzi ndi Loti ndipo tidawaika ku dziko limene tidalidalitsa kuti zolengedwa zonse zikhalemo
Ndipo Ife tidamupatsa Isake ndi Yakobo ngati chidzukulu chake ndipo tidawapanga onse kukhala anthu angwiro
Ndipo Ife tidawasankha iwo kukhala atsogoleri olangiza anthu ku ulamuliro wathu ndipo tidawalamulira kuti azigwira ntchito zabwino ndipo, azipitiriza kupemphera ndi kupereka zothandizira osauka. Ndipo iwo anali kutitumikira Ife nthawi zonse
Ndi Loti tidamupatsa luntha, utumiki ndi nzeru za chipembedzo ndipo tidamupulumutsa ku mzinda umene anthu ake anali kuchita zoipa. Ndithudi, iwo anali anthu ochita zoipa ndipo anali osamvera Mulungu
Ndipo Ife tidamulowetsa m’chisomo chathu, ndithudi, iye adali mmodzi wa anthu olungama
Ndi pamene Nowa adatipempha poyamba, Ife tidamva pempho lake ndipo tidamupulumutsa iye pamodzi ndi anthu ake ku chilango choopsa
Ndiponso Ife tidamupulumutsa ku gulu la anthu amene adakana chivumbulutso chathu. Ndithudi iwo anali anthu oipa ndipo onse tidawamiza m’madzi
Pamene Davide ndi Solomoni adaweruza mulandu wa munda umene nkhosa zosochera za anthu ena zidadya nthawiyausiku. Ndipo Ifetidalimbonipachiweruzochawo
Ife tidapatsa Solomoni nzeru zoweruzira nkhaniyi ndipo aliyense wa iwo tidamupatsa luntha, utumwi ndi nzeru. Tinalamula mapiri ndi mbalame kuti zikhale pamodzi ndi Davide pomutamanda Mulungu. Ndife amene tidachita zonsezi
Ndipo tidamuphunzitsa luso lopanga zovala za nkhondo kuti zizikutetezani pa nthawi ya nkhondo, Kodi ndinu othokoza
Ndi Solomoni, Ife tidampeputsira mphamvu ya mphepo. Iyo inali kuomba potsatira malamulo ake kupita kudziko limene Ife tidalidalitsa. Ndipo Ife timadziwa zinthu zonse
Ndipo pakati pa a Satana padali ena omwe amaimira m’malo mwa iye ndipo amachitanso ntchito zina. Kuonjezera apa ndipo ndife amene timawayang’anira iwo
Ndi Yobu pamene adaitana Ambuye wake nati, “Ine, ndithudi, mavuto andikuta ndipo Inu ndinu wachisoni kuposa achisoni onse.”
Motero Ife timamuyankha pempho lake ndipo tidamuchotsera mavuto ake ndipo tidamubwezeranso banja lake ndi zinthu zambiri zimene tidamupatsa ngati chisomo chochokera kwa Ife ndi chikumbutso kwa onse amene amatipembedza Ife
Ndipo Ishimayeli, Idris ndi dhulkifl, onse adali anthu opirira
Ndipo Ife tidawalowetsa m’chisomo chathu. Ndithudi iwo adali anthu olungama
Ndi dhan-Nun pamene adachoka mokwiya kwambiri chifukwa iye adali kuganiza kuti Ife sitingamulenge iye. Koma mu mdima iye adaitana, “Kulibe Mulungu wina koma Inu nokha. Ulemerero ukhale kwa Inu! Ndithudi ine ndidali mmodzi mwa anthu olakwa!”
Motero Ife tidayankha pempho lake ndipo tidamupulumutsa ku mavuto ake. Motero ndimo mmene timapulumutsira anthu okhulupirira
Ndi Zakariya pamene anaitana Ambuye wake nati, “Ambuye wanga! Musandileke ndekha. Ndipo Inu ndinu wabwinomwaokhalitsaonse.”
Motero Ifetidamuyankha pempho lake ndipo tidamupatsa Yohane ndipo tidathetsa uchumba wa mkazi wake. Ndithudi iwo adali ofulumira pochita ntchito zabwino ndipo amatipempha Ife ndi chikhulupiriro ndi mantha ndiponso amadzichepetsa kwa Ife
Adali mkazi amene adasunga unamwali wake. Ife tidauzira mwa iye ndipo tidamupanga iye pamodzi ndi mwana wake wa mwamuna kukhala chizindikiro kwa zolengedwa zonse
Ndithudi! Ichi ndi chipembedzo chanu ndipo ndi chipembedzo chimodzi, ndipo Ine ndine Ambuye wanu motero ndipembedzeni Ine ndekha
Ndipo iwo adapatukana ndi kugawa chipembedzo chawo pakati pawo ndipo ndi kwa Ife kumene adzabwerera
Motero aliyense amene achita ntchito zabwino ndipo ndi wokhulupirira moona ntchito zake sizidzakanidwa ayi. Ndithudi Ife timazilemba zonse m’Buku la chiwerengero
Ndipo ndi koletsedwa kuti mudzi umene tidawuwononga kuti ubwererenso
Mpaka pamene anthu a Ya-juj ndi Majuj adzamasulidwa ndipo iwo adzakhala akutsika kuchokera kumalo aliwonse wokwera
Ndipo pamene lonjezo loona lidzafika, maso a anthu onse osakhulupirira adzapenyetsetsa mwamantha nati “Tsoka kwa ife! Ndithudi ife tidali osalabadira zimenezi. Zoonadi ife tidali ochita zoipa.”
Ndithudi! Inu pamodzi ndi zimene mukupembedza kuonjezera pa Mulungu, mudzakhala nkhuni za ku Gahena! Kumeneko nonse mudzalowako
Iyo ikadakhala milungu, siikadalowa kumeneko ndipo onse adzakhala kumeneko
Kumeneko iwo adzalira ndipo adzakhala osamva
Ndithudi iwo amene tawaonetsera chifundo chathu, iwo adzakhala kutali ndi moto
Iwo sadzamva mkokomo wake pamene iwo ali kumene mitima yawo imafuna mpaka kalekale
Zoopsa sizidzawadandaulitsa ayi ndipo Angelo adzawalandira iwo nati,“Ili ndi tsiku lanu limene inu mudalonjezedwa.”
Tsiku limene tidzapinde thambo monga momwe timapindira tsamba la Buku. Monga momwe tidayamba chilengedwe choyamba momwemonso tidzachibwezeranso. Ili, ndithudi, ndi lonjezo kwa Ife. Ndithudi, Ife, tidzachita motero
Ndipo, ndithudi, Ife tidalemba m’Buku la Masalimo, motsatira chikumbutso kuti akapolo anga angwiro adzakhala ku dziko lapansi
Ndithudi mu ili muli Uthenga womveka kwa anthu amene amapembedza Mulungu
Ndipo sitidakutumize iwe pa chifukwa china koma ngati madalitso kwa zolengedwa zonse
Nena, “Zavumbulutsidwa kwa ine kuti Mulungu wanu ndi mmodzi yekha. Kodi inu mudzadzipereka kwa Iye?”
Koma ngati iwo safuna kumvera nena, “Ine ndili kukuchenjezani kuti tonse tidziwe. Ine sindidziwa kuti chimene mwalonjezedwa chidza msanga kapena chikadali patali.”
Ndithudi Mulungu amadziwa zonse zimene mumayankhula mokweza ndipo amadziwanso zimene mubisa
Ndipo ine sindidziwa ngati awa ndi mayeso kwa inu ndi chisangalalo cha kanthawi kochepa
Iye anati, “Ambuye wanga! Weruzani mwachilungamo! Ambuye wathu ndi Mwini chisoni chosatha amene chithandizo chake chimafunika pa zimene inu muonjezera.”
oh anthu inu! opani Ambuye wanu ndipo kwaniritsani udindo wanu kwa Iye. Ndithudi chivomezi cha nthawiyo chidzakhala choopsa kwambiri
Tsiku limene mudzachiona, mkazi aliyense woyamwitsa adzaiwala mwana wake ndipo mkazi aliyense wapakati adzabala nthawi yake isanafike ndipo udzawaona anthu ngati oledzera pamene sali oledzera; koma chilango cha Mulungu chidzakhala chowawa
Ndipo pakati pa anthu pali ena amene amatsutsa za Mulungu pamene sazidziwa, ndipo amatsatira Satana aliyense ogalukira
Kwa iye, zidalamulidwa kuti aliyense amene amutsatira iye, adzamusocheretsa ndipo adzamupititsa ku chilango cha ku ng’anjo ya moto
Oh anthu inu! Ngati inu mukayika za kuukanso kwa akufa, ndithudi, Ife tidakulengani kuchokera ku dothi, ndi kudontho la umuna, losakanizana ndi ukazi ndiponso kuchokera ku mnofu oumbidwa bwino osonyeza ziwalo za munthu ndi wina mnopfu umene siunayambe kusonyeza ziwalo kuti tikusonyezeni mphamvu zathu. Ndipo Ife timakhazikitsa m’chiberekero cha mkazi chilichonse chimene tifuna panthawi yomwe yaikidwa ndipo timakutulutsani ngati makanda ndipo mumakula kufika pa msinkhu waumunthu. Ndipo ena a inu amafa ndipo ena amabwezeredwa moyo wapansi kuti asadziwe zonse zimene anali kudziwa kale. Ndipo inu mumaona nthaka ili youma yosamera chilichonse koma tikatsitsa madzi panthakapo, iyo imayamba kugwedezeka ndi kutupa ndi kumeretsa mbewu zokongola zamitundumitundu
Zimenezo ndi chifukwa chakuti Mulungu ndiye choonadi ndipo Iye amapereka moyo ku zinthu zakufa ndipo ali ndi mphamvu pa chinthu china chilichonse
Ndithudi ola lili nkudza mosakayika pamene Mulungu adzawadzutsa onse amene ali m’manda
Ndipo pakati pa anthu pali wina amene amatsutsa za Mulungu pamene sakudziwa chilichonse ndiponso chilangizo kapena Buku la chivumbulutso
Munthu wotere amathyola khosi monyadira ndi kusocheza ena ku njira ya Mulungu. Kwa otere kuli mnyozo m’moyo uno ndipo patsiku louka kwa akufa, tidzamulawitsa chilango cha moto woyaka
“Izi ndi chifukwa cha zomwe manja anu adatsogoza ndipo, ndithudi, Mulungu sapondereza akapolo ake
Ndipo pakati pa anthu pamakhala munthu amene amampembedza Mulungu mokayikira. Zikapezeka zabwino amakhala wokhutitsidwa ndi izo koma ngati mavuto amugwera amatembenuka motero; iye amataya zabwino za m’moyo uno ndi za m’moyo umene uli nkudza. Kumeneko ndiko kulephera koonekeratu
Iwo amapempha mowonjezera pa Mulungu, zimene sizingathe kumuononga kapena kumuthandiza. Kumeneko ndiko kusochera kwenikweni
Amapempha kwa iye amene mavuto ake ali pafupi kuposa chithandizo chake. Iye, ndithudi, ndi mtsogoleri woipa ndiponso bwenzi loipa
Ndithudi Mulungu adzawalowetsa onse amene amakhulupilira ndipo amachita ntchito zabwino m’minda yothiriridwa ndi mitsinje ndi madzi oyenda. Ndithudi Mulungu amachita zimene afuna
Ngati wina aganiza kuti Mulungu sadzathandiza Mtumwi wake m’dziko lino ndi m’dziko limene lili nkudza, mulekeni amange chingwe ku phaso la nyumba yake ndi kudzimangirira yekha. Ndipo mulekeni kuti awone yekha ngati cholinga chake chingachotse vuto lomwe limamukwiyitsa iye
Kotero Ife talitumiza ilo ngati zizindikiro zooneka ndipo ndithudi Mulungu amatsogolera aliyense amene Iye wamufuna
Ndithudi iwo amene amakhulupirira, ndi iwo amene ndi Ayuda, Masabina, Akhirisitu, a Magiyani ndi akunja, ndi iwo amene amapembedza zinthu zina mowonjezera pa Mulungu. Ndithudi, Mulungu adzawaweruza pa tsiku la kuuka kwa akufa ndipo Mulungu ndi mboni pa zinthu zonse
Kodi iwe siudaone kuti zinthu zonse zimalambira Mulungu mwachitsanzo zinthu zimene zimakhala kumwamba ndi padziko lapansi monga dzuwa, mwezi, nyenyezi, mapiri mitengo, nyama ndi anthu ambiri? Koma pali ambiri amene chilango ndi chowayenera. Aliyense amene achititsidwa manyazi ndi Mulungu, palibe wina amene angamulemekeze. Ndithudi! Mulungu amachita zimene afuna
Awa awiri otsutsana, akutsutsana za Ambuye wawo ndipo akakhala sakhulupirira Mulungu, adzawasokera zovala za ku moto ndipo madzi ogaduka adzathiridwa paliombo pawo
Ndi iwo zidzasungunuka zonse zimene zili m’mimba mwawo ndi pa makungu pawo
Iwo adzamangidwa ku unyolo wa zitsulo
Nthawi iliyonse imene azidzafuna kuti athawe m’menemo, chifukwa chaululu, azidzabwezedwa momwemo ndipo adzauzidwa kuti, “Lawani chilango chamoto.”
Ndithudi Mulungu adzawalowetsa anthu okhulupirira ndi ochita ntchito zabwino, m’minda yothiriridwa ndi mitsinje yoyenda. Iwo adzavekedwa zibangiri za golide ndi mphete za nkhombe ndipo zovala zawo zidzakhala za silika
Iwo ndi otsogozedwa ndi mawu abwino ndipo adatsogozedwa ku njira ya Iye amene ayenera kutamandika kwambiri
Ndithudi! Iwo amene sakhulupirira ndipo amaletsa anzawo kutsatira njira ya Mulungu ndi kupita ku Mzikiti woyera umene tidaupereka kwa anthu a mitundu yonse, kaya ndi eni dziko kaya ndi alendo chimodzimodzi ngati amachita zoipa m’kati mwake, tidzamulawitsa chilango chowawa
Ndi pamene tidamulangiza Abrahamu malo omangapo Mzikiti Woyera tidamuuza kuti, “Usapembedze wina aliyense koma Ine ndekha. Ndipo yeretsa nyumba yanga kuti izikhala yaukhondo chifukwa cha anthu amene amayenda kuizungulira iyo ndi iwo amene amaimirira kapena amagwada ndi kuwerama popembedza.”
Ndipo uza anthu onse kupita ku Hajji. Iwo adzadza kwa iwe poyenda ulendo wapansi kapena atakwera ngamira yowonda chifukwa chakutopa ndipo iwo adzadza kuchokera kumbali zonse za kutali ndi njira za m’mapiri
Kuti adzaona zinthu zimene zili zaphindu kwa iwo ndi kutchula dzina la Mulungu, pa masiku osankhidwa, pa nyama ya ng’ombe imene Iye wawapatsa iwo. Idyani gawo lina ndiponso dyetsani osauka amene ali pa mavuto
Aloleni kuti amalize miyambo yofunika ndi kukwaniritsa malonjezo awo ndiponso kuzungulira Nyumba ya Makedzana
Izi zikhale choncho. Ndipo aliyense amene alemekeza miyambo yolemekezeka ya Mulungu zidzakhala zabwino kwa iye pamaso pa Ambuye wake. Nyama ya ng’ombe, ndi yololedwa kwa inu kupatula nyama zokhazo zimene zikutchulidwa kwa inu kukhala zoletsedwa. Pewani zonyansa za mafano, ndipo pewani bodza
Musapembedze wina aliyense koma Mulungu ndipo musatumikire milungu ina. Aliyense amene amatumikira milungu ina yoonjezera pa Mulungu weniweni, ali ngati iye amene agwa kuchokera kumwamba, ndipo asanagwe pansi, amalandiridwa ndi mbalame kapena kunyamulidwa ndi mphepo kukam’taya kumalo akutali
Zimenezi zili tero. Aliyense amene amalemekeza zizindikiro za Mulungu kumeneko ndiko kuyera mtima
Mu izo muli zokoma zosiyanasiyana mpaka pa nthawi imene yaikidwa ndipo pomaliza zimaperekedwa ngati nsembe ku Nyumba ya Makedzana
Ku mtundu uliwonse, Ife tidakhazikitsa miyambo yachipembedzo kuti azitchula dzina la Mulungu pa nyama zimene Iyeadawapatsaiwongatichakudya. Ndipo Mulungu wanu ndi Mulungu mmodzi yekha motero muzigonjera Iye yekha. Auzeni nkhani yabwino anthu onse odzichepetsa
Anthu amene mitima yawo imadzala ndi mantha pamene Mulungu atchulidwa ndiponso amene amapilira pamavuto amene awapeza ndipo amapitiriza mapemphero awo ndi kupereka zina za zimene tidawapatsa
Ndi nyama zina tidazipanga kukhala ngati zina mwa zizindikiro za Mulungu ndipo mwa izo muli zofunika kwambiri kwa inu. Motero tchulani dzina la Mulungu pa izo pamene muziika kuti ziperekedwe nsembe. Ndipo zikaphedwa, idyani nyama yake ndiponso mumudyetse wopempha ndi amene apempha mwamanyazi. Kotero Ife nyamazi tazipereka kwa inu kuti mukhale othokoza
Si mnofu wawo kapena magazi awo amene amafika kwa Mulungu koma ndi kumvera Mulungu kumene kumafika kwa Iye. Kotero Ife tazilamula kuti zizikutumikirani kuti muzilemekeza Mulungu chifukwa chokulangizani inu njira yoyenera. Auze nkhani yabwino anthu angwiro
Ndithudi Mulungu amatchinjiriza anthu okhulupirira. Ndithudi Iye sakonda anthu a chinyengo ndiponso osathokoza
Chilolezo chomenya nkhondo chili kuperekedwa kwa iwo amene aputidwa, chifukwa chakuti awachimwira. Ndithudi Mulungu ali ndi mphamvu yowapambanitsa
Anthuwo ndi amene apirikitsidwa kuchokerakunyumbazawomopandachilungamochifukwa chakuti iwo anati, “Ambuye wathu ndi Mulungu.” Ndipo Mulungu akadapanda kuyesa anthu ena ndi mphamvu za anthu anzawo makachisi, matchalitchi, masunagoge ndi mizikiti imene dzina la Mulungu limatchulidwa kwambiri ikadaonongekeratu. Ndithudi Mulungu adzathandiza amene amathandiza chipembedzo chake. Ndithudi Mulungu ndi mphamvu ndiponso Wopambana kwambiri
Iwo amene tawapatsa mphamvu padziko lapansi adzapitiriza mapemphero nthawi zonse ndi kupereka msonkho wothandiza osauka, ndipo adzakhazikitsa chilungamo ndi kuletsa zoipa. Kwa Mulungu ndiko kuli mapeto a zinthu zonse
Ndipo ngati akukana iwe, ndithudi asanadze awa, nawonso anthu a Nowa, Aad ndi Thamud adakana Atumwi awo
Ndiponso anthu a Abrahamu ndi anthu a Loti zidali choncho
Ndi anthu okhala ku Midiyani. Mose nayenso adakanidwa. Koma Ine ndidawapatsa nthawi anthu osakhulupirira ndipo pomaliza chilango changa chidawapeza onse. Kodi chilango changa chidali choopsa bwanji
Kodi ndi mizinda ingati ya anthu ochita zoipa imene taononga? Mizinda yawo idaonongeka, madenga ake kugwera pansi ndiponso ndi zitsime zingati zimene zidangokhala kusowa anthu otungapo madzi ndiponso ndi nyumba zingati zomangidwa bwino zimene zidasanduka mabwinja
Kodi iwo sanayende pa dziko kuti mitima yawo ikhale yozindikira ndi makutu awo kuti amvere? Ndithudi si maso awo amene ali ndi khungu, koma ndi mitima imene ili mu zifuwa zawo imene ili ndi khungu
Ndipo ali kuuza iwe kuti ufulumizitse chilango! Ndipo Mulungu salephera kukwaniritsa lonjezo lake. Ndithudi tsiku lililonse kwa Mulungu lili ngati zaka chikwi chimodzi mu kuwerenga kwanu
Ndi mizinda ingati imene ndidaipatsa mwayi wa nthawi pamene iyoyo inali kuchitabe zoipa? Ndipo pambuyo pake ndidaipatsa chilango Kwa Ine zinthu zonse zidzabwerera
Nena, “Oh anthu inu! Ndithudi ine ndatumizidwa ngati mchenjezi wanu!”
Motero iwo amene akhulupirira ndi kuchita ntchito zabwino, adzakhululukidwa machimo awo ndi kulipidwa mphotho yolemekezeka
Koma iwo amene amalimbikira kutsutsa zizindikiro zathu, adzakhala eni ake a ku Gahena
Ife sitidatumizepo Mtumwi kapena Mneneri, iwe usanadze, koma iye amati akamalakatula chivumbulutso kapena kulalikira, Satana anali kuonjezera bodza. Koma Mulungu amachotsa zonse zimene Satana waikamo. Motero Mulungu amakhazikitsa chivumbulutso chake ndipo Mulungu ndi wodziwa ndi waluntha
Kuti Iye apange zimene wanena Satana kukhala mayesero kwa iwo amene m’mitima mwawo muli matenda ndi amene mitima yawo ndi youma. Ndithudi anthu ochita zoipa amatsutsa kwambiri choonadi
Ndipo kuti iwo amene adapatsidwa nzeru azindikire kuti ichi ndi choonadi chochokera kwa Ambuye wako ndipo ayenera kukhulupirira ndi kuti mitima yawo ikhale yodzichepetsa chifukwa cha iyo. Ndithudi Mulungu ndi Mtsogoleri wa iwo amene akhulupirira njira yoyenera
Ndipo anthu osakhulupirira adzapitirira kukayikira chivumbulutso mpaka pamene ora lomaliza lidzawapeza mwadzidzidzi kapena mpaka pamene chilango cha tsiku louka kwa akufa chidzawadzera
Ufumu, patsiku limeneli, udzakhala wa Mulungu yekha. Iye adzaweruza pakati pawo. Motero onse amene adakhulupirira ndipo amachita ntchito zabwino adzakhala ku Paradiso
Ndipo iwo amene sanakhulupirire ndipo amakana zizindikiro zathu chawo chidzakhala chilango chochititsa manyazi
Iwo amene adasamuka kwawo chifukwa chofuna kukweza chipembedzo cha Mulungu ndipo pambuyo pake adaphedwa kapena adafa, Mulungu, ndithudi, adzawapatsa mphatso zabwino. Ndithudi Mulungu ndi wopereka zabwino kuposa onse amene amapereka
Ndithudi Mulungu adzawalowetsa iwo ku malo amene adzasangalala nawo ndipo Mulungu, ndithudi, ndi wodziwa zonse ndiponso wopirira kwambiri
Izo zili tero. Ndipo aliyense amene abwezera mnzake chilango chofanana ndi chimene iye wapatsidwa ndipo pambuyo pake amulakwiranso, ndithudi, Mulungu adzamuthandiza iye. Ndithudi! Mulungu ndi wachisoni ndiponso wokhululukira
Ichi ndi chifukwa chakuti Mulungu amalowetsa usiku mu usana ndi kulowetsa usana mu usiku. Ndithudi Mulungu ndi wakumva ndi woona
Zonsezi ndi chifukwa chakuti Mulungu ndiye choonadi ndipo zonse zimene iwo amazipembedza kuonjezera pa Mulungu ndi zabodza. Ndithudi Mulungu ndi wapamwamba ndiponso wamkulu
Kodi iwe siukuona kuti Mulungu amagwetsa mvula kuchokera kumwamba ndipo kuti nthaka imakhala ndi zomera zobiriwira? Ndithudi Mulungu ndi Mwini chisoni chosatha, wodziwa zonse zobisika ndi zoonekera
Mulungu ndiye mwini zonse za kumwamba ndi dziko lapansi. Ndithudi Mulungu ndi wolemera ndi wotamandidwa
Kodi inu simuona kuti Mulungu wakupeputsirani zonse zimene zili pa dziko lapansi ndi zombo zimene mumayendera pa nyanja ndi chilolezo chake? Iye amagwira thambo kuti lisagwe pansi. Ndithudi Mulungu ndi wachisoni ndiponso wachifundo kwa anthu
Iye ndiye amene adakupatsani moyo ndipo adzapangitsa kuti mufe ndi kukupatsaninso moyo kachiwiri. Ndithudi munthu ndi wosathokoza
Ku mtundu uliwonse Ife tidalamulira miyambo ya chipembedzo imene iwo ayenera kuitsatira ndipo iwo asakangane ndi iwe pa nkhani iyi. Koma aitanire kwa Ambuye wako. Ndithudi iwe uli pa njira yoyenera
Ndipo ngati iwo atsutsana ndi iwe, nena “Mulungu amadziwa bwino zonse zimene inu mumachita.”
Mulungu adzaweruza, pakati panu, patsiku lachiweruzo, zimene inu munali kusiyana
Kodi iwe siudziwa kuti Mulungu amadziwa zonse zimene zili kumwamba ndi pa dziko lapansi? Ndithudi zonse zidalembedwa m’Buku lake. Ndithudi zimenezo ndi zosavuta kwa Mulungu
Ndipo iwo ali kupembedza zinthu zina mowonjezera pa Mulungu, zinthu zimene sanapatsidwe umboni kuti azizigwadira ndipo ndi zimene iwo salikuzindikira. Ndithudi, anthu ochimwa alibe wowathandiza
Ndipo pamene chivumbulutso chathu chomveka chilakatulidwa kwa iwo, iwe udzaona kukana pa maso pa anthu osakhulupirira! Iwo ali pafupifupi kumenyana ndi iwo amene amalakatula chivumbulutso chathu kwa iwo. Nena “Kodi mufuna ndikuuzeni zoipa kuposa chizindikiro choterechi? Chizindikirocho ndi moto wa ku Gahena umene Mulungu walonjeza anthu osakhulupirira ndipo amenewa ndi malo oipa kupitako.”
Oh anthu inu! Fanizo laperekedwa ndipo limvetsetseni. Ndithudi! Iwo amene mumawapembedza kuonjezera pa Mulungu weniweni sangathe kulenga ntchentche imodzi ngakhale onse atagwirizana kuti achite choncho. Ndipo ngati ntchentche italanda kalikonse kuchokera kwa iwo, iwo sangathe kuilanda ayi. Anthu opempha ndi wopemphedwa onse alibe mphamvu
Iwo sapereka ulemu kwa Mulungu umene uyenera kuperekedwa kwa Iye. Ndithudi Mulungu ali ndi mphamvu ndipo ndi Mwini mphamvu zonse
Mulungu amasankha Atumwi ake pakati pa Angelo ndi pakati pa anthu. Ndithudi Mulungu amamva zonse ndiponso amaona chilichonse
Iye amadziwa zonse zimene zili patsogolo pawo ndi zimene zili m’mbuyo mwawo. Kwa Mulungu zinthu zonse zimabwerera
oh inu anthu amene mwakhulupirira! weramani ndipo gunditsani mphumi zanu pansi ndi kupembedza Ambuye wanu ndipo chitani ntchito zabwino kuti mupambane
Ndipo limbikani kwambiri chifukwa cha chipembedzo chaMulungumongammenezikufunikira.Iyewakusankhani inu ndipo sadakukundikireni mavuto muchipembedzo chanu. Chipembedzo cha Abrahamu atate wanu. Iye ndiye amene akupatsani inu dzina lakuti Asilamu kuyambira kalekale ndiponso mu dzinali Mtumwi ndiye mboni yanu, ndipo nanunso mukhale mboni ya anthu anzanu. Pitirizani mapemphero, perekani msonkho wothandizira anthu osauka ndipo khulupirirani mwa Mulungu. Iye ndi Mtetezi wanu wabwino ndiponso Mthandizi wabwino kwambiri
Anthu okhulupirira ndiwo opambana
Iwo amene amadzichepetsa akamapemphera
Ndi iwo amene amalewa nkhani zabodza
Ndipo amapereka zaulere kwa anthu osauka
Ndi iwo amene amadziteteza ku chiwerewere
Kupatula kwa akazi awo kapena akapolo awo akazi, chifukwa iwo sangadzudzulidwe
Koma amene angafune zina pamwamba pa zimene tawaloleza anthu otere ndi ochimwa
Amene amakwaniritsa malonjezo ndi mapangano awo
Ndi iwo amene amasunga mapemphero awo
Amenewa ndithudi ndiwo amene adzalowa
Iwo adzalowa ku Paradiso ya pamwamba ndipo adzakhalamo mpaka kalekale
Ndithudi Ife tidapanga munthu kuchokera ku dothi labwino
Titatero tidamukonza iye kukhala dontho la umuna m’malo otetezedwa mu msana
dontho la umunali tidalipanga kukhala dontho la magazi ndipo dontho lamagazili tidalipanga kukhala m’bulu wa mnofu. Ndipo mnofu umenewu tidaukonza kukhala mafupa ndipo tidakuta mafupa ndi mnofu. Kotero tidamupanga iye kukhala chilengedwe china. odalitsa akhale Mulungu, Namalenga wabwino kwambiri mwa onse
Ndipo pambuyo pake inu nonse mudzafa
Ndipo mudzapatsidwanso moyo patsiku la kuuka kwa akufa
Ife tidalenga miyamba isanu ndi iwiri pamwamba panu ndipo kwa zolengedwa zathu. Ndipo Ife sitikhala osalabadira ayi
Ife timatumiza madzi kuchokera kumwamba m’muyeso wokwana ndipo timawalowetsa pansi pa nthaka. Ndipo Ife tili ndi mphamvu yowachotsa madziwo
Ndipo Ife timakutulutsirani mmenemo minda ya tende ndi mphesa, m’mene muli zipatso zanu zambiri zimene zina mwa izo mumadya
Mtengo umene umamera pa phiri la Sinai, umapereka mafuta ndiponso ndiwo kwa anthu
M’nyama namonso muli chizindikiro choonetsa mphamvu zathu. Inu timakumwetsani zimene zili m’mimba mwake ndipo mumadya nyama yake ndiponso mumapeza phindu lambiri
Ndipo pa izo ndi m’zombo zimene zimayenda pa nyanja, inu mumanyamulidwa
Tidamutumiza Nowa kwa anthu ake ndipo iye adati, “Tumikirani Mulungu anthu anga chifukwa mulibe mulungu wina koma Iye yekha. Kodi simungamuope Iye?”
Akuluakulu osakhulupirira a anthu ake adati, “Munthu uyu ndi wolingana ndi inu, iye ali kungodziyenereza kuti ndi wopambana pakati panu.” Mulungu akadafuna, akadatumiza angelo. Ndiponso zinthu za mtundu uwu sitidamvepo kuchokera kwa makolo athu akalekale
Ndithudi ameneyu ndi wopenga, ndipo mumuyang’anire pa kanthawi.”
Iye adati, “Ambuye! Ndithandizeni ine chifukwa iwo ali kundikana.”
Ife tidavumbulutsa chifuniro chathu kwa iye ponena kuti, “Khoma chombo chimene Ife tidzayang’anira molingana ndi chilangizo chathu. Pamene chiweruzo chathu chidza ndipo madzi asefukira kuchokera ku ng’anjo, utenge zolengedwa ziwiriziwiri, zazimuna ndi zazikazi ndiponso kuchokera kwa iwo a m’nyumba mwako kupatula okhawo amene adanenedwa kuti adzaonongeka. Usandipemphe kuti ndipulumutse iwo amene adachita zoipa chifukwa iwo adzamizidwa.”
Ndipo pamene iwe ndi iwo amene akutsata iwe mulowa m’chombo, nena, “Kuyamikidwa kukhale kwa Mulungu amene watipulumutsa ife kuchoka ku mtundu wa anthu oipa.”
Ndipo nena: “Ambuye wanga! Ndithandizeni kuti ndikafike pamalo podalitsika chifukwa Inu ndinu wabwino wa onse amene amafikitsa pamalo okocheza.”
Ndithudi mu zimenezi muli zizindikiro zooneka. Ndithudi Ife timawaika anthu m’mayesero
Potero Ife tidapanga mtundu wa anthu a tsopano pambuyo pawo
Ndipo tidatumiza kwa iwo Mtumwi wa mtundu wawo amene adati, “Tumikirani Mulungu chifukwa inu mulibe mulungu wina koma Iye yekha. Kodi simungamuope Mulungu?”
Koma akuluakulu a anthu osakhulupirira a anthu ake, amene adakana za moyo umene uli nkudza ndi amene tidawapatsa zinthu zabwino za m’moyo uno adati, “Munthu uyu ndi munthu monga inu nomwe amene akudya zimene mumadya inu ndi kumwa zimene inu mumamwa.”
“Ngati inu mumvera munthu wonga inu nomwe, ndithudi, inu mudzatayika.”
“Kodi iye ali kukuopsezani kuti pamene inu mutafa ndi kusanduka dothi ndi mafupa mudzadzuka ndi kukhalanso ndi moyo?”
“Zimene inu muli kuopsezedwa nazo zili kutali.”
“Kulibenso moyo wina koma moyo wathu wapadziko lapansi basi. Ife timafa ndi kukhala ndi moyo ndipo ife sitidzadzukanso ayi.”
“Munthu uyu ndi odziyenereza amene ali kunena za Mulungu zimene sizili zoona ayi. Ife sitidzamukhulupirira.”
Iye adati, “Ambuye! Ndithandizeni ine chifukwa iwo ali kunditsutsa.”
Iye adati, “Posachedwapa iwo adzanong’oneza bombono.”
Chilango chathu chidawapeza mwachilungamo ndipo tidawafafaniza monga zinyalala. Chionongeko kwa anthu onse ochimwa
Atapita awa tidalenganso mitundu ina ya anthu
Palibeanthuameneangafulumizitsekapenakuchedwetsa chionongeko chawo
Ndipo Ife tidatumiza Atumwi ena motsagana ndipo nthawi iliyonse Mtumwi amadza kwa iwo ndipo amamukana nati ndi wabodza. Ndipo Ife tidawaononga ena pambuyo pawo ndipo tidawapanga iwo kukhala chitsanzo cha mbiri ya anthu olakwa. Ichi chidali chionongeko cha anthu osakhulupirira
Ndipo Ife tidamutumiza Mose pamodzi ndi m’bale wake Aroni ndi zizindikiro ndiponso ulamuliro wathu
Kwa Farawo ndi nduna zake ndipo iwo adawalandira mwamwano chifukwa iwo adali anthu a chipongwe
Ndipo iwo adati, “Kodi ife tikhulupirire anthu awiri olingana ndi ife amene anthu awo ndi akapolo athu?”
Iwo adawakana iwo kotero iwo adalandira chionongeko
Ndipo Ife tidamupatsa Mose Buku la Chipangano Chakale kuti anthu ake akhoza kutsogozedwa bwino
Ife tidamupanga mwana wamwamuna wa Maria pamodzi ndi amayi ake kukhala chizindikiro kwa anthu onse ndipo tidawapatsa mnthunzi pa malo okwera ndi malo a mtendere amene anali kuthiriridwa ndi madzi a pa kasupe
Oh Atumwi! Idyani zinthu zabwino ndipo muzichita ntchito zabwino. Ndithudi Ine ndimadziwa zonse zimene mumachita
Ndithudi chipembedzo chanu ndi chimodzi ndipo Ine ndine Ambuye wanu. Kotero ndiopeni Ine
Koma anthu adagawanika m’magulu osiyanasiyana, gulu lililonse limasangalala ndi ziphunzitso zawo
Alekeni ayambe achimwa mpaka pamene imfa iwapeza
Kodi iwo amaganiza kuti popeza tawapatsa chuma ndi ana
Ndiye kuti Ife tili kuwafunira zabwino? Iyayi. Iwo sadziwa kanthu ayi
Ndithudi iwo ndi anthu amene amaopa Ambuye wawo
Amene amakhulupirira zizindikiro za Ambuye wawo
Amene sapembedza wina aliyense poonjezera pa Ambuye wawo
Amene amapereka chaulere mitima ili yoopa Ambuye wawo chifukwa chakuti adzabwerera kwa Iye
Awa ndiwo amene amapikisana wina ndi mnzake pochita zabwino ndipo amakhala oyamba pozindikira
Ife sitinyamulitsa mzimu wina uliwonse katundu amene iwo sangathe kunyamula. M’buku lathu mudalembedwa zoona zokhazokha. Ndipo palibe munthu amene adzaponderezedwa
Koma mitima ya anthu osakhulupirira siyizidziwa zimenezi ayi. Iwo ali ndi ntchito zina zoipa kupatula zimene iwo amachita
Koma pamene chilango chathu chidza pa iwo amene amakhala mu mtendere, iwo adzafuula kufuna chithandizo
Musalire tsiku la lero chifukwa inu simudzalandira chithandizo china chilichonse kuchokera kwa Ife
Chivumbulutso changa chinali kulakatulidwa kwa inu nthawi zambiri koma inu munali kuthawa ndi kuchikana mwamwano
Inu mumachinyoza usana ndi usiku uliwonse
Kodi iwo sangathe kulingalira mozama pa mawu a Mulungu kapena pali china chake chimene chidavumbulutsidwa kwa iwo chimene sichidavumbulutsidwe kwa makolo awo
Kapena iwo sadziwa kuti akukana Mtumwi wawo
Kapena iwo akuti Iye ndi wopenga? Koma iye wawabweretsera iwo onse zoonadi. Koma ambiri amakana choonadi
Kukadakhala kuti choonadi chimatsatira zofuna zawo, ndithudi, kumwamba, dziko lapansi ndi onse okhala m’menemo akadaonongeka. Ife tawapatsa chikumbutso komabe iwo safuna kumvera chikumbutsocho
Kapena iwe uli kuwapemphera mphotho? Chithandizo cha Ambuye wawo ndicho chabwino. Ndipo Iye ndiye wopereka moolowa manja kuposa onse amene amapereka
Ndithudi iwe uli kuwaitana kuti adze kunjira yoyenera
Ndithudi iwo amene amakana moyo umene uli nkudza adzakhala ali kusochera ku njira yoyenerayi
Ngati Ife tikadawalangiza chisoni chathu ndi kuwachotsera mavuto, iwo akadakhala ali kulakwabe m’njira zawo zoipa ndi kusokonezeka ndi zoipazo
Ndithudi tidawalanga kale koma iwo sadafunefune Ambuye wawo kapena kukhala odzichepetsa pamaso pake
Mpaka pamene tidzawatsekulira khomo la chilango chowawa, iwo adzakhala okhumudwa
Iye ndiye amene adakupatsani makutu, maso ndi mitima. Komabe inu simuthokoza mokwanira
Iye ndiye amene adakulengani ndi kukuchulukitsani padziko lapansi ndipo nonsenu mudzasonkhanitsidwa kudza pamaso pake
Iye ndiye amene amapereka moyo ndiponso imfa ndipo ndi Iyenso amene amasithanitsa usiku ndi usana. Kodi simungazindikire
Iwo amanena zimene anthu akale ankanena
Iwo amati, “Pamene ife tafa ndi kusanduka dothi ndi mafupa, kodi tidzadzukanso ndi kukhala ndi moyo?”
Ndithudi ife tidalonjedzedwa zimenezi kale pamodzi ndi makolo athu. Izi si zina ayi koma nkhani zabodza za anthu a makedzana
Nena, “Kodi Mwini wake wa dziko lapansi ndi zonse zimene zili mmenemo ndani? Ndiuzeni ngati mumudziwa.”
Iwo adzati, “Mwini wake ndi Mulungu.” Nena, “Kodi inu simungachenjezedwe?”
Nena, “Kodi Ambuye wa miyamba isanu ndi iwiri ndiponso Mwini Ufumu ndani?”
Iwo adzati, “Mwini wake ndi Mulungu.” Nena, “Nanga kodi simungasiye kuchita zoipa?”
Nena, “Kodi ulamuliro wa zinthu zonse zili m’manja mwa yani? Kodi ndani amene amaziteteza zonse pamene Iye safuna chitetezo cha wina aliyense ngati inu mukudziwa?”
Iwo adzati, “M’manja mwa Mulungu.” Nena, “Nanga ndi chifukwa chiyani inu mwanyengedwa?”
Iyayi, Ife tawavumbulutsira choonadi. Koma onsewa ndi anthu abodza
Palibe nthawi imene Mulungu adabala mwana ndipo kulibe Mulungu wina woonjezera pa Iye. Ngati izi zikadakhala choncho, bwezi Mulungu aliyense akumatenga zolengedwa zake zokha ndi kumaziika pamwamba pa zolengedwa za Mulungu wina. Ulemerero ukhale kwa Mulungu woposa zina zilizonse
Iye amadziwa zonse zooneka ndiponso zobisika. Mulungu akhale wopambana milungu ina imene iwo amaitumikira
Nena, “Ambuye wanga! Ngati Inu mukadandionetsa chilango chimene muli kuwopseza
Ambuye wanga! Pulumutsani ndipo musandisiye ine pakati pa mtundu wa anthu oipawu.”
Ndithudi, Ife tili ndi mphamvu zoti ukhoza kuona chilango chimene tawaopseza
Dzitetezeni ndi chabwino pothamangitsa choipa. Ife tili kudziwa zonse zimene ali kukunamizirani
Ndipo iwe unene kuti, “Ambuye wanga, Ine ndili kufuna chitetezo chanu pothawa zoipa za Satana.”
“Ambuye! Ine ndili kupempha chitetezo chanu kuti asabwere kumene ndili ine.”
Mpaka pamene imfa idza kwa munthu wolakwa iye adzati, “Ambuye wanga! Bwezeni.”
“Kuti ndikachite ntchitozabwinozimenendidalepherakuchita.” Kosatheka! Amenewa ndiwo mawu chabe amene akungolankhula. Kumbuyo kwawo kudzakhala chipupa mpaka pa tsiku la kuuka kwa akufa
Ndipo pamene lipenga lidzaombedwa, pa tsiku limeneli, ubale wawo wonse udzathera pomwepo ndiponso sadzafunsana chithandizo chochokera kwa wina ndi mnzake
Aliyense amene muyeso wake udzakhala wolemera, adzapambana
Koma aliyense amene muyeso wake udzakhala wopepuka adzataya moyo wake ndipo adzakhala ku Gahena nthawi zonse
Moto udzatentha nkhope zawo ndipo izo zidzakwinyikakwinyika chifukwa chaululu
“Kodi chivumbulutso chathu sichidalakatulidwe kwa inu? Kodi simudachikane?”
Iwo adzati, “Ambuye wathu! Zilakolako zathu zidatigonjetsa ife ndipo tidali anthu osochera.”
“Ambuye wathu! tipulumutseni ife ku ichi. Ngati ife tidzabwereranso ku zoipa, ndithudi, ife tidzakhala anthu oipa kwambiri.”
Iye adzati, “Khalani mu icho mwamanyazi ndipo musandiyankhulitse Ine ayi.”
Ndithudi padali gulu la Atumiki anga amene adati, “Ambuye wathu! Ife timakhulupirira mwa inu. Tikhululukireni ndipo mutichitire chisoni. Inu ndinu wabwino pochita chisoni kuposa a chisoni onse.”
Koma inu munali kuwanyogodola mpaka pamene inu mudandiiwala Ine ndipo inu munali kuwaseka iwo
Ndithudi lero Ine ndawalipira chifukwa cha kupirira kwawo ndipo iwo ndi amene apambana
Ndipo Iye adzafunsa kuti, “Kodi inu munakhala padziko lapansi zaka zingati?”
Iwo adzayankha kuti, “Takhala tsiku limodzi kapena mphindi zochepa zokha. Afunseni iwo amene amasunga chiwerengero.”
Iye adzawayankha kuti, “Inu mukadadziwa ndi nthawi yochepa kwambiri imene inu munakhala.”
“Kodi inu mumaganiza kuti tidangokulengani inu opanda cholinga ndipo kuti simudzabwerera kwa Ife?”
Motero alemekezeke Mulungu, Mfumu ya chilungamo. Palibe Mulungu wina koma Iye yekha, Ambuye wa Mpando wolemekezeka ndi Wachifumu
Aliyense amene apembedza mulungu wina woonjezera pa Mulungu, pamene Iye alibe umboni wa chimenecho, Ambuye wake adzamufunsa. Ndithudi anthu osakhulupirira sadzapambana ayi
Nena, “Ambuye wanga! Ndikhululukireni machimo anga ndipo mundichitire chisoni chifukwa Inu ndinu wachisoni choposa a chisoni onse.”
Ife tavumbulutsa mutu uwu ndipo taupanga kukhala wokakamiza ndipo ndi mwa iwo mmene tavumbulutsa chivumbulutsochoonekakutiinumukhozakuchenjezedwa
Munthu wamkazi wosakwatiwa akachita chigololo ndi munthu wamwamuna wosakwatira, mukwapule aliyense wa iwo zikoti zana limodzi ndipo musalole kuti chifundo chikulepheretseni kumvera lamulo la Mulungu ngati inu mumakhulupirira mwa Mulungu ndi tsiku lomaliza. Ndipo onetsetsani kuti chilango chawo chachitidwa umboni ndi anthu ambiri okhulupirira
Mwamuna wachigololo asakwatire wina koma mkazi wachigololo kapena mkazi wopembedza mafano. Mkazi wachigololo asakwatiwe ndi wina koma mwamuna wachigololo kapena wopembedza mafano. Anthu okhulupirira moona saloledwa maukwati otere
Iwo amene amanamizira akazi odzisunga kuti achita chigololo ndipo sangathe kutulutsa mboni zinayi, akwapulidwe zikoti makumi asanu ndi atatu. Mukane umboni wawo mpaka kalekale. Anthu otere ndi oononga
Kupatulaokhawoamene, patapitanthawi, alapandikusiya makhalidwe awo onyansa. Mulungu ndi wokhululukira ndi Mwini chisoni chosatha
Ndipo ngati mwamuna akuti mkazi wake wachita chigololo koma alibe mboni kupatula iye mwini, iye alumbire kanayi dzina la Mulungu kuti zimene ali kunena ndi zoona
Ndipo kachisanu anene kuti matemberero a Mulungu akhale pa iye mwamunayo ngati ali kunama
Koma ngati mkazi wake alumbira kanayi, potchula dzina la Mulungu, kutsutsa kuti zimene ali kunena mwamuna wake ndi zabodza, sadzalandira chilango
Ndipo kachisanu ayenera kunena kuti mkwiyo wa Mulungu ukhale pa iye mkaziyo ngati ali kunama
Pakadapanda chisoni ndi chisomo cha Mulungu mukadaonongeka. Ndithudi Mulungu ndi wokhululukira ndi waluntha
Iwo amene adapeka nkhani yabodzayi, adali gulu la anthu anu omwe. Usaganize kuti ndi masoka koma ndi zabwino kwa inu. Aliyense adzalangidwa molingana ndi tchimo lake. Akakhala iye amene amaikulitsa nkhaniyi, chilango chake chidzakhala chowawa kwambiri
Pamenemudamvankhaniyi, bwanjianthuokhulupirira, amuna ndi akazi, sadafune kuganizira zabwino za anthu awo ndi kunena kuti, “Ili ndi bodza loonekera poyera?”
Kodi ndi chifukwa chiyani iwo sadabweretse mboni zinayi? Ngati iwo adalephera kutulutsa mboni ndiye kuti iwo anali kunama pamaso pa Mulungu
Kukadakhala kuti Mulungu sadaonetse chisomo ndi chifundo chake pa inu, m’moyo uno ndiponso m’moyo umene uli nkudza, mukadalangidwa kwambiri chifukwa cha zimene mwakhala mukuchita
Pamene inu munali kunena ndi malirime anu ndiponso kuyankhula ndi pakamwa panu zinthu zimene simunali kuzidziwa, inu munali kuganiza kuti izi zidali zopepuka koma pamaso pa Mulungu zinali zazikulu
Pamene mudazimva, bwanji inu simudanene kuti, “Si koyenera kuti ife tikambe izi ayi. Mulungu ayeretsedwe! Kumeneku ndiko kunama kwenikweni.”
Mulungu ali kukuchenjezani kuti musadzachitenso izi ngati inu ndinu anthu okhulupirira m’choonadi
Mulungu ali kukufotokozerani momveka chivumbulutso chake. Iye ndi wanzeru ndipo amadziwa zonse
Iwo amene amasangalala kuti nkhani zoipa zokhudza anthu okhulupirira zifalikire, adzalangidwa kwambiri m’moyo umene uli nkudza. Mulungu ali kudziwa zonse pamene inu simudziwa
Pakadakhala popanda chisomo cha Mulungu kwa inu, nonse mukanaonongedwa. Ndithudi Mulungu ndi wabwino ndiponso wachisoni
oh inu anthu okhulupirira m’choonadi! Musatsatire mapazi a Satana. Aliyense amene atsatira mapazi a Satana, ndithudi, iye amalamulira zinthu zochititsa manyazi ndi zoipa. Koma pakadapanda chisomo cha Mulungu, panalibe wina wa inu amene akadayeretsedwa zoipa zake. Koma Mulungu amayeretsa aliyense amene Iye wamufuna. Mulungu amamva zonse ndiponso amadziwa chinthu china chilichonse
Musalole kuti anthu olemera ndi olemekezeka amene ali pakati panu kuti alumbire kuti sadzapereka chithandizo kwa abale awo, kwa anthu osauka ndiponso kwa iwo amene adathawa ku midzi yawo chifukwa cha nkhani zokhudza Mulungu. Iwo ayenera kuwakhululukira ndi kuwalekerera. Kodi inu simufuna kuti Mulungu akukhululukireni? Mulungu ndi Mwini chikhululukiro ndiponso Mwini chisoni chosatha
Onse amene amaipitsa mbiri ya akazi odzisunga ndiponso okhulupirira amene sachita zoipa, adzakhala otembereredwa m’dziko lino ndiponso mulimene lili nkudza. Chawo chidzakhala chilango choopsa
Patsikuli malirime awo, manja awo, ndi miyendo yawo zidzachitira umboni pa zimene iwo anali kuchita
Patsiku limeneli Mulungu adzawapatsa dipo lawo loyenera, ndipo iwo adzadziwa kuti Mulungu ndiye choonadi chenicheni
Zinthu zodetsedwa ndi zoyenera anthu odetsedwa ndipo zinthu zosadetsedwa ndi za anthu osadetsedwa, ndiponso zinthu zabwino ndi zoyenera anthu abwino. Kotero anthu abwino ndi oyenera zinthu zabwino ndipo anthu otere sakhudzidwa ndi zimene akunena; iwowa adzakhululukidwa ndipo adzapatsidwa mphotho yolemekezeka
Oh inu anthu okhulupirira! Musalowe m’nyumba za anthu ena pokhapokha mutapempha chilolezo cha eni ake ndipo alonjereni powafunira iwo mtendere. Zimenezo ndi zabwino kwa inu kuti muchenjezedwe
Mukapeza kuti kulibe aliyense, musalowe mpaka pokhapokha mwapatsidwa chilolezo. Ngati akuuzani kuti mubwerere kapena musalowe, ndi chilungamo kuti inu mubwerere kupita komwe mwachokera. Zimenezo ndi zabwino kwa inu. Mulungu amadziwa zonse zimene mumachita
Sichidzakhala cholakwa ngati inu mulowa m’nyumba zopanda okhalamo zomwe muli nazo ndi ntchito. Mulungu amadziwa zonse zimene mumaulula ndi zimene mumabista
Auze amuna okhulupirira kuti azitsitsa maso awo ndi kulewa chigololo. Zimenezi ndizo zimene zidzayeretsa moyo wawo. Mulungu amadziwa zonse zimene mumachita
Auze akazi okhulupirira kuti azitsitsa maso awo ndipo asachite chiwerewere ndiponso azibisa zinthu zimene zimawakongoletsa kupatula zokhazo zimene sizingabisike. Ndipo azifunda nsalu kumutu ndi pa chifuwa chawo ndiponso asaonetse kukongola kwawo kupatula kwa amuna awo, abambo awo, abambo a amuna awo, ana awo aamuna, ana a amuna awo, ana a chemwali awo kapena ana a achimwene awo kapena ana a alongo awo kapena akazi anzawo owakhulupirira; ndiponso antchito awo aakazi, a ntchito awo a amuna ndi ana amene alibe chilakolako cha akazi. Ndipo iwo asamamenyetse mapazi awo pansi akamayenda ndi cholinga choonetsa zina zokongola zawo zobisika. Oh inu okhulupirira! Lapani kwa Mulungu mogonja kuti mupambane
Kwatiranani ndi iwo a pakati panu amene ndi osakwatiwa ndiponso akapolo anu aamuna kapena aakazi amene ali olungama. Ngati iwo ndi osauka, Mulungu adzawalemeretsa iwo kuchokera ku zabwino zake. Mulungu ndiye wopatsa ndi wodziwa
onse amene sangathe kukwatira adzisunge mpaka pamene Mulungu awapatsa iwo zabwino zake. Akakhala a kapolo anu amene afuna kugula ufulu wawo, amasuleni ngati inu muona kuti iwo ndi abwino ndipo muwapatseko gawo la chuma chimene Mulungu wakupatsani inu. Inu musadzakakamize akapolo anu aakazi kuti azichita chiwerewere ngati iwo afuna kudzisunga ndi cholinga chofuna kupeza zinthu zabwino za padziko lapansi. Ngati wina aliyense awakakamiza iwo, Mulungu adzawakhululukira ndi kuonetsa chisoni chake pa iwo
Ife takutumizirani inu chivumbulutso chooneka bwino ndipo takupatsani chitsanzo cha anthu amene adalipo kale ndi chilangizo kwa anthu angwiro
Mulungu ndi Muuni wa kumwamba ndi dziko lapansi. Kuunika kwake kukhoza kufaniziridwa ndi malo olowa m’chipupa amene m’kati mwake muli nyali imene ili m’galasi looneka ngati nyenyezi yowala. Iyo imayatsidwa kuchokera ku mtengo wodalitsika wa Azitona umene siuli kum’mawa kapena kumadzulo. Mafuta ake amatha kuwala ngakhale kuti palibe moto owayakitsa mafutawo. Muuni pa Muuni unzake ndipo Mulungu amatsogolera, ndi kuwala kwake, aliyense amene Iye wamufuna. Mulungu amapereka zitsanzo kwa anthu. Ndipo Mulungu amadziwa chilichonse
M’nyumba zimene Mulungu adalamula kuti zimangidwe ndipo m’menemo dzina lake limakumbukirika, Mulungu amalemekezeka m’menemo m’mawa ndi madzulo
Pali anthu amene malonda kapena zogulitsa sizingathe kuwaiwalitsa kukumbukira Mulungu kapena kupemphera kapena kupereka msonkho wothandiza anthu osauka. Iwo amene amaopa tsiku limene mitima ndi maso adzatembenuka
Kotero Mulungu adzawalipira chifukwa cha ntchito zawo zabwino ndiponso adzawapatsa zabwino zochokera m’chisomo chake. Mulungu amapereka mopanda muyeso kwa aliyense amene Iye wamufuna
Akakhala anthu osakhulupirira, ntchito zawo zili ngati chizirezire cha m’chipululu. Wapaulendo amene ali ndi ludzu amaganiza kuti ndi madzi koma akachiyandikira amaona kuti palibe chilichonse. Iye amamupeza Mulungu pomwepo amene amamupatsa molingana ndi ntchito zake. Mulungu amachita chiwerengero cha zinthu mofulumira
Kapena monga mdima wa m’nyanja yozama kwambiri yokutidwa ndi mafunde aakulu oyenda pamwamba pa mafunde anzake ndi mitambo pamwamba pake ndiponso mdima wosanjana ndi mdima unzake. Ndipo ngati iye atambasula dzanja lake sangathe kuliona. Ndithudi munthu amene saunikidwa ndi Mulungu sangathe kuona kuwala kwa mtundu wina uliwonse
Kodi iwe siunaone kuti zonse zimene zili kumwamba ndi pa dziko la pansi zimalemekeza Mulungu ndiponso pamene mbalame zikutambasula mapiko ake? Chilichonse chimadziwa mapemphero ndi mayamiko omupatsa Iye ndipo Mulungu amadziwa ntchito zawo zonse
Ndipo Mulungu ndiye mwini ufumu wa kumwamba ndi wa padziko lapansi. Ndi kwa Mulungu kumene zinthu zonse zidzabwerera
Kodi inu simuona mmene Mulungu amayendetsera mitambo? Ndipo amaisonkhanitsira ndi kuiika m’gulu limodzi ndipo inu mumaona mvula ili kuchokera mu mitamboyo. Kuchokera ku mapiri a kumwamba, Iye amatumiza mphepo kuti ipeze kumupeza wina aliyense amene wamufuna ndi kusiya aliyense amene wamufuna. Chilangali cha mphenzi zake chimakhala pang’ono kuti chilande maso a anthu
Mulungu amasanduliza usiku ndi usana. Ndithudi mu izi muli chizindikiro kwa anthu ozindikira
Mulungu adalenga cholengedwa chilichonse kuchokera ku madzi ndipo zina zimayenda chafufumimba, zina zimayenda ndi miyendo iwiri ndi zina zimayenda ndi miyendo inayi. Mulungu amalenga chilichonse chimene wafuna. Ndithudi Mulungu ali ndi mphamvu pa chinthu china chilichonse
Ndithudi Ife tatumiza chivumbulutso choonetsa choonadi. Ndipo Mulungu amalangiza aliyense amene Iye wamufuna ku njira yoyenera
Iwo amanena monenetsa kuti, “Ife timakhulupirira mwa Mulungu ndi Mtumwi wake ndipo timawamvera onsewa.” Koma pambuyo pake ena a iwo amabwerera m’mbuyo. Ndithudi awa si okhulupirira ayi
Ndipo pamene iwo amaitanidwa kuti adze kwa Mulungu ndi Mtumwi wake, kuti akhoza kuwaweruza, ena amakana
Chikadakhala kuti choonadi chili mwa iwo, iwo akadadza kwa iye modzipereka
Kodi m’mitima mwawo muli matenda kapena ali ndi chikayiko? Kapena iwo amaopa kuti Mulungu ndi Mtumwi wake akhoza kuwakaniza chiweruzo cholungama? Koma oterewa ndi ochita zoipa
Koma pamene anthu okhulupirira enieni amaitanidwa kwa Mulungu ndi Mtumwi wake kuti akhoza kuwaweruza, yankho lawo limangokhala lakuti, “Tamva ndipo titsatira.” Anthu otere ndiwo opambana
Ndipo iye amene amvera Mulungu ndi Mtumwi wake ndi kuopa Mulungu ndipo amadzichepetsa kwa Iye, oterewa ndi opambana
Iwo amalumbira pali Mulungu molimba kuti ngati iwe uwalamulira kumenya nkhondo, adzakumvera iwe. Nena “Musalumbire ayi! Chofunika ndi kumvera basi. Ndithudi Mulungu amadziwa chilichonse chimene mumachita.”
Nena “Mverani Mulungu ndipo mverani Mtumwi wake. Ngati simungamvere, iye ali ndi udindo wake monga momwe inu muli ndi udindo wanu. Ngati inu mumumvera, inu mudzatsogozedwa ndipo udindo wa Mtumwi ndi kungopereka uthenga womveka.”
Mulungu walonjeza ena a inu amene akhulupirira ndipo amachita ntchito zabwino kuti adzawasandutsa kukhala olowa m’malo padziko monga momwe adasandutsira anthu amene adalipo kale iwo asanadze. Ndipo Iye adzawapatsa mphamvu yoyendetsa chipembedzo chawo chimene adawasankhira. Ndithudi Iye adzawapatsa m’malo mwake chitetezo chokwana atawachokera mantha ngati iwo andipembedza Ine ndipo sandiphatikiza ndi china chilichonse. Ndipo onse amene sakhulupirira atamva izi ndi ochimwa
Kwaniritsani mapemphero anu, perekani msonkho wothandiza osauka, ndipo muzimvera Mtumwi kuti mupeze chisomo cha Mulungu
Musaganize kuti anthu osakhulupirira adzathawa mdziko lino. Moto ndi imene idzakhala mudzi wawo. Ndipo kutsiliza koipa
oh inu anthu okhulupirira! Lolani akapolo anu aamuna ndi aakazi ndi ana amene sanathe msinkhu kuti apemphe poyamba pa nthawi zitatu, musadapemphere pemphero la m’mawa kapena pamene mwavula zovala zanu masana chifukwa cha kutentha kapena mutatha kupemphera mapemphero a usiku. Izi ndi nthawi zitatu zokhala panokha. Palibe chifukwa kwa inu kapena kwa iwo kuchezerana, wina ndi mnzake mu nthawi zina kupatula nthawi zimene zatchulidwazi. Kotero Mulungu amaulula poyera chivumbulutso chake kwa inu. Ndipo Mulungu ndi Wodziwa ndi Waluntha
Ndipo pamene ana akula msinkhu, alekeni kuti apemphe chilolezo chanu monga akuluakulu awo amachitira. Kotero ndi mmene Mulungu amaululira chivumbulutso chake kwa inu. Ndipo Mulungu ndi wodziwa ndi waluntha
Sichidzakhala cholakwa kwa amayi okalamba amene alibe maganizo a ukwati ngati angasiye zovala zawo zakunja popanda kuonetsa kukongola kwawo. Kungakhale bwino ngati iwo angavale modzilemekeza. Ndipo Mulungu ndi wakumva ndi wodziwa
Si cholakwa ngati munthu wakhungu kapena wolumala kapena wodwala kapena inu eni ake mudya m’nyumba zanu kapena m’nyumba za atate anu kapena m’nyumba za amayi anu kapena m’nyumba za achimwene anu kapena m’nyumba za alongo anu kapena m’nyumba za achimwene a atate anu kapena alongo awo atate anu kapena m’nyumba za amalume anu kapena m’nyumba za achemwali a amayi anu kapena m’nyumba zimene makiyi ake mwasunga kapena aliyense m’nyumba za abwenzi anu. Palibe cholakwa kwa inu ngati mudya pamodzi kapena payekha payekha. Pamene mulowa m’nyumba, lonjeranani wina ndi mnzake malonje odalitsika ochokera kwa Mulungu. Kotero Mulungu ali kukufotokozerani zizindikiro kuti mukhoza kukhala ozindikira
Ndi okhawo amene ali ndi chikhulupiriro, amene amakhulupirira mwa Mulungu ndi Mtumwi wake ndipo amati akasonkhana pamodzi ndi iye pa zinthu zofunika sachoka mpaka pamene apempha chilolezo chake. Ndithudi anthu amene amakupempha chilolezo ndiwo amene amakhulupirira mwa Mulungu ndi Mtumwi wake. Pamene akupempha iwe chilolezo choti achoke ndi cholinga chokagwira ntchito zawo, pereka chilolezo kwa aliyense amene iwe wamufuna ndipo mumupemphe Mulungu kuti awakhululukire machimo awo. Mulungu amakhululukira ndipo ndi wachisoni chosatha
Musamuitane Mtumwi pomutchula dzina monga momwe mumaitanirana wina ndi mnzake. Mulungu amadziwa ena a inu amene amazemba ndi kuchoka pakati panu. Aleke onse amene samvera Mtumwi kuti achenjere mwina mayesero kapena chilango chowawa chikhoza kugwa pa iwo
Ndithudi mwini wake wa chilichonse chimene chili kumwamba ndi dziko lapansi ndi Mulungu. Ndithudi Iye amadziwa zonse zimene zili m’mitima mwanu. Ndipo patsiku limene iwo adzabwerera kwa Iye, Iye adzawauza zonse zimene amachita. Ndipo Mulungu amadziwa chinthu china chilichonse
Alemekezeke Iye amene adavumbulutsa Korani kwa Mtumwi wake kuti akhoza kuchenjeza mitundu ya anthu
Iye ndiye Mfumu ya kumwamba ndi dziko lapansi. Iye ndiye amene sadabereke mwana ndipo alibe wothandizana naye mu Ufumu wake. Iye ndiye amene adalenga zinthu zonse ndipo adakhazikitsa mmene zili ndi mapeto ake
Komabe anthu osakhulupirira amapembedza milungu ina yoonjezera pa Mulungu weniweni imene siingathe kulenga china chilichonse chifukwa chakuti nayonso idachita kulengedwa. Ndi imene singathe kuwathandiza kapena kuwaononga ndiponso imene ilibe mphamvu pa nkhani zokhudza imfa kapena moyo kapena kuukitsa anthu akufa
Anthu osakhulupirira amanena kuti, “Zonsezi ndi zinthu zabodza zimene wapeka yekha, ndiponso anthu ena amamuthandiza. Zonse zimene watulutsa ndi zopanda pake ndipo zabodza
Ndipo iwo amati, “Izi ndi nkhani zopanda pake za anthu amakedzana zimene iye walemba. Izo zimalembetsedwa kwa Iye m’mawa ndi masana aliwonse.”
Nena, “Wavumbulutsa ndiye amene amadziwa zinsinsi za kumwamba ndi za padziko lapansi. Iye amakhululukira ndipo ndi Mwini chisoni chosatha.”
Iwo amanena kuti, “Uyu, ndi Mtumwi wotani amene amadya ndipo amayendayenda ku msika? Kodi bwanji mngelo sanathe kutumizidwa pansi pamodzi ndi iye kudzatichenjeza ife?”
“Nanga ndi chifukwa chiyani sadapatsidwe chuma ndipo alibe munda woti azipezako chakudya?” Ndipo anthu ochita zoipa amati, “Ndithudi munthu amene muli kumutsatira ndi wolodzedwa.”
Taona mafanizo amene amakupatsa iwe! Iwo asochera ndipo sangathe kubwerera kunjira yoyenera
Alemekezeke Iye amene, ngati afuna akhoza kukupatsa iwe zinthu zabwino kuposa zimenezi monga minda yothiriridwa ndi madzi a m’mitsinje ndi nyumba zachifumu
Iyayi. Iwo amakana ola lachiweruzo, ndipo iwo amene amakana olali, Ife tawakonzera moto woyaka
Pamene idzawaona iwo kuchokera kutali, iwo adzamva mkokomo wake
Ndipo onse akadzamangidwa limodzi, adzaponyedwa kumalo opanikizika. Ndithudi iwo adzafuna imfa itadza pa iwo
Lero musaitane imfa imodzi yokha ayi koma itanani imfa zambiri
Nena, “Kodi chimenecho ndi chabwino kapena Paradiso yosatha imene anthu angwiro adalonjezedwa?” Imeneyo ndiyo mphotho yawo ndi kobwerera kwawo
Iwo adzapeza m’menemo zonse zimene anali kufuna ndi kukhala momwemo. Limenelo ndilo lonjezo limene ndi lofunika kumapempha pafupipafupi kuchokera kwa Ambuye wako
Patsiku limene Iye adzawasonkhanitsa onse ndi zomwe amapembedza kuonjezera pa Mulungu weniweni ndipo Iye adzati, “Kodi ndinu amene munasocheza akapolo anga kapena ndi iwo okha anasochera ku njira yoyenera?”
Iwo adzati, “Ulemerero ukhale kwa Inu! Si koyenera kwa ife kuti tisankhe otisamalira ena oonjezera pa Inu. Koma Inu mudawapatsa iwo ndi makolo awo zinthu zokoma za dziko, kotero kuti iwo adaiwala chenjezo lanu ndipo adali anthu oonongeka.”
Kotero iwo adatsutsa mawu anu ndipo inu simungathe kuthawa kapena kupeza chithandizo ndipo aliyense amene ndi wosalungama pakati panu, Ife tidzamupatsa chilango chachikulu
Ife sitidatumizepo Atumwi kale amene sanali kudya ndi kuyenda m’misika. Ife tidakupangani ena a inu kukhala mayesero a ena. Kodi simungapirire? Ambuye wanu amaona chilichonse
Iwo amene alibe chikhulupiriro choti adzakumana ndi Ife amati, “Kodi ndi chifukwa chiyani angelo sadatumizidwe kwa ife? Kapena ndi chifukwa chiyani kuti ife sitingaone Ambuye wathu?” Ndithudi iwo adadzikweza kwambiri
Patsiku limene iwo adzaona angelo, anthu ochita zoipa sadzasangalala ayi ndipo iwo adzati, “Ambuye wathu! Ikani malire pakati pa ife ndi iwo.”
Ndipo Ife tidzabweretsa zonse zimene adachita ndikuzionetsa kuti ndi zinthu zopanda ntchito ngati fumbi louluka
Anthu okhala ku Paradiso, adzakhala kumalo abwino patsiku limeneli ndiponso malo abwino opumulako
Patsiku limeneli kumwamba pamodzi ndi mitambo yake idzagawanika pakati ndipo angelo adzatumizidwa pansi pano m’maudindo awo
Patsiku limeneli ufumu wonse udzakhala wa Mwini chisoni chosatha. Limeneli lidzakhala tsiku lovuta kwambiri kwa anthu osakhulupirira
Patsiku limeneli munthu ochita zoipa adzanong’oneza bombono nati, “Oh zikadakhala bwino ndikadakhala kuti ndidatsatira zimene Mtumwi anali kunena!”
“oh kalanga ine! Ndikadakhala kuti sindidasankhe a uje ndi a uje kuti akhale anzanga!”
“Mosakayika ndiwo amene adandisokoneza ine kuti ndisakhulupirire machenjezo a Mulungu pamene machenjezowo atandifika. Ndithudi Satana ndi wachinyengo nthawi zonse kwa munthu.”
Mtumwi adati, “Ambuye wanga! Ndithudi anthu anga alikana Buku la Korani.”
Motero Ife tapanga kwa Mtumwi aliyense mdani kuchokera kwa anthu ochimwa, anthu otsutsana naye, ndipo Ambuye wako ali wokwana kukhala wokutsogolera mu zabwino ndiponso ngati wokuthandiza wako
Anthu osakhulupirira anati, “Kodi ndi chifukwa chiyani Korani yonse siidavumbulutsidwe kwa iye nthawi imodzi?” Ife talivumbulutsa kotero kuti tikhoza kulimbikitsa mtima wako ndipo takupatsa ilo kwa iwe mu chivumbulutso chapang’onopang’ono
Iwo sadzatha kubwera ndi mtsutso umene Ife sitidakonze yankho loona ndi kafotokozedwe kake
Iwo adzaduduluzidwa cha mphumi kupita ku Gahena ndipo iwo adzakhala ndi malo oipa okhalamo ndipo njira yawo ndi yosochera
Ndithudi Ife tidavumbulutsa mawu a Mulungu kwa Mose ndipo tidamupatsa m’bale wake Aroni kuti akhale nduna yomuthandiza
Tidawauza iwo kuti, “Pitani nonse kwa anthu amene adakana zizindikiro zathu” ndipo pambuyo pake tidawaononga kotheratu
Akakhala anthu a Nowa, tidawamiza pamene iwo adakana Atumwi awo ndipo tidawapanga iwo kukhala phunziro kwa anthu a mitundu yonse. Ndipo anthu ochimwa tawakonzera chilango chowawa
Mitundu ya anthu a ku Thamoud ndi Aad nawonso tidawaononga ndiponso iwo amene anali kukhala ku Raas ndi mibadwo yochuluka imene idadza pakati pawo
Ndipo onsewa, tidawapatsa zitsanzo ndipo onse tidawaononga kotheratu
Ndithudi anthu osakhulupirira adadutsa pa mzinda umene udaonongeka ndi madzi a mvula. Kodi iwo sadauone mzindawu? Komabe iwo adalibe chikhulupiriro mu kuukanso kwa akufa
Nthawi zonse akakuona iwe amakunyoza ndipo amati, “Kodi uyu ndiye munthu amene akuti Mulungu wamutumiza ngati Mtumwi wake?”
Ngati ife tikadapanda kulimba popembedza milungu yathu ndithudi iye akadatitembenuza ife kuti tisiye milungu yathu. Koma posakhalitsa iwo adzaona chilango ndipo adzadziwa kuti ndani amene adasochera kwambiri
Kodi wamuona iye amene amayesa zilakolako zake ngati milungu? Kodi iwe ungakhale munthu wosamalira munthu wotere
Kodi iwe umaganiza kuti ambiri a iwo angathe kumva kapena kuzindikira? Iwo si chinthu china chilichonse koma ali ngati nyama yosochera kwambiri
Kodi iwe siuona mmeneAmbuye wako amatambasulira mthunzi? Mulungu akadafuna, akadaupanga kuti ukhale wokhazikika. Ndipo Ife tapanga dzuwa kukhala chizindikiro chake
Ndipo timaubweretsa kwa Ife mwapang’onopang’onomosavuta
Ndiyeamenewapanga usiku kukhala chofunda ndi tulo kuti tikhale mpumulo, ndipo wapanga usana kuti uzikhala nthawi yodzuka ndi kumagwira ntchito
Ndiye amene amatumiza mphepo ngati mthenga wobweretsa chisomo chake ndipo timatumiza madzi abwino kuchokera kumwamba
Ndi cholinga choti tipereke moyo ku nthaka imene inali yakufa ndi kuti timwetse zinthu zimene talenga, nyama ndi anthu ambiri
Ndithudi tawatumizira pakati pawo, kuti akhoza kukumbukira, chisomo cha Mulungu koma anthu ambiri amakana. Ndipo iwo amasankha kusakhulupirira
Chikadakhala chifuniro chathu, tikadautsa wowachenjeza ku mzinda uliwonse
Iwe usawamvere anthu osakhulupirira koma limbana nawo kwambiri pogwiritsa ntchito Korani ino
Ndiye amene adatumiza nyanja ziwiri, ina yamadzi ozuna ndi abwino pamene ina ndi yamadzi a mchere ndi owawa ndipo adakhazikitsa malire olimba kwambiri pakati pa nyanjazi
Ndiye amene adamulenga munthu kuchokera ku madzi ndipo adamupatsa abale chifukwa cha magazi amodzi ndiponso chifukwa cha ukwati. Ndipo Ambuye wako ndiye mwini mphamvu zonse ndipo amachita zimene afuna
Komabe anthu osakhulupirira amapembedza mafano moonjezerapa Mulungu Mafanowosangathekuwathandiza kapena kuwaononga. Munthu wosakhulupirira amathandiza Satana kuchita zoipa zosakomera Ambuye wake
Ndipo takutumiza iwe ngati wobweretsa nkhani yabwino ndiponso munthu wopereka chenjezo
Nena, “Ine sindili kukupemphani malipiro pa ntchito iyi ayi kupatula kuti iye amene afuna atsatire njira yoyenera yopita kwa Ambuye wake.”
Ndipo ika chikhulupiriro chako mwa Iye wa moyo amene sakufa ayi. Ndipo mulemekeze nthawi zonse. Iye ndi okwana chifukwa Iye amadziwa bwinobwino za machimo a akapolo ake
Iye adalenga kumwamba ndi dziko lapansi ndi zonse zimene zili m’menemo masiku asanu ndi limodzi. Ndipo atatero adabuka pa chimpando chaufumu, Mwini Chisononi chosatha. Motero mufunse Iye chifukwa amadziwa china chili chonse
Pamene zimanenedwa kwa iwo kuti, “Lambirani Mwini chisoni chosatha,” Iwo amati; “Kodi Mwini chisoni chosatha ndani? Kodi iwe ufuna kuti ife tizipembedza chilichonse chimene iwe utilamula?” Mawu amenewa amaonjezera kukana kwawo
Alemekezeke Iye amene adalenga gulu la nyenyezi kumtambo ndipo adalenga dzuwa ndi mwezi wowala
Ndipo ndiye amene amasinthanitsa usiku ndi usana chifukwa cha iye amene afuna kukumbukira kapena afuna kuonetsa kuyamika kwake
Ndipo akapolo a Mwini Chisoni Chosatha ndi iwo amene amayenda modzichepetsa padziko lapansi ndipo ngati mbuli zikawayankhula mwachipongwe iwo amayankha mwaulemu
Ndipo iwo amene amachezera pamaso pa Ambuye wawo, amagwada ndi kuima
Amene amanena kuti, “Ambuye wathu! Tichotsereni chilango cha ku Gahena.” Ndithudi chilango chake ndi chosatha
Ndithudi kumeneko ndi malo wonyansa kupumirako ndiponso malo wonyansa kukhalako
Iwo akamapereka saononga chuma chawo moposa muyeso ndipo saumira koma amakhala pakatikati
Ndipo anthu amene sapembedza mulungu wina kuonjezera pa Mulungu weniweni ndipo sakupha mzimu umene Mulungu waletsa kupatula mu njira yachilungamo ndipo sachita chigololo. Ndipo aliyense amene achita izi adzalandira chilango
Chilango chake chidzaonjezedwa kawiri patsiku la kuuka kwa akufa ndipo adzakhala ndi manyazi nthawi zonse
Kupatula okhawo amene alapa ndi kukhulupirira ndi kuchita ntchito zabwino, chifukwa potero Mulungu adzasintha zoipa zawo kukhala ntchito zabwino. Ndipo Mulungu amakhululukira ndi wachisoni chosatha
Iye amene alapa ndi kuchita ntchito zabwino, ndithudi, ndiye kuti wabwerera kwa Mulungu
Iwo amene sapereka umboni ku zinthu zabodza ndipo akamadutsa pamalo pamene pakuchitika zinthu zoipa kapena zoletsedwa, iwo amadutsa modzilemekeza
Amene sanyozera chivumbulutso cha Ambuye wawo ndipo pamene akumbutsidwa za icho sachita ngati kuti iwo ndi a gonthi kapena a khungu
Ndipo anthu amene amanena kuti, “Ambuye wathu! Tipatseni chisangalalo mu akazi ndi ana athu ndipo tipangeni ife kukhala atsogoleri a iwo amene amakuopani Inu!”
Amenewa adzalipidwa Paradiso wa pamwamba chifukwa cha kupirira kwawo. Kumeneko adzalandiridwa ndi malonje abwino mawu amtendere ndi aulemu
Adzakhala kumeneko nthawi zonse ndipo ndi malo abwino kukhalako ndiponso ndi malo abwino opumirako
Nena “Ambuye wanga amakusamalani inu chifukwa cha mapempheroanuakwa Iyeyekha. Komatsopano, ndithudi, inu mwamukana Iye. Motero chilango chidzakhala chanu mpaka kalekale.”
Ta Sin Mim
Awa ndi mawu omveka a Buku la Korani
Iwe mwina ukhoza kudziononga ndi madandaulo chifukwa cha kusakhulupirira kwawo
Ngati Ife tifuna, tikhoza kuwavumbulutsira chizindikiro chochokera kumwamba chimene makosi awo adzakhota modzichepetsa
Palibe chenjezo latsopano limene limadza kuchokera kwa Mwini chisoni chosatha koma iwo amalikana
Ndithudi iwo amakana mawu a Mulungu koma nkhani zidzadza kwa iwo zokhudza zinthu zimene iwo amazichita chipongwe
Kodi iwo saona nthaka, mmene ife tameretsamo mbewu zabwino zosiyanasiyana
Ndithudi m’menemu muli chizindikiro komabe ambiri a iwo sakhulupirira ayi
Ndithudi Ambuye wako ndiye Mwini mphamvu zonse ndiponso Mwini chisoni chosatha
Ndipo pamene Ambuye wako adamuitana Mose adanena kuti, “Pita kwa anthu opanda chilungamo.”
Kodi anthu a Farawo sangaope
Iye adati, “Ambuye wanga! Ndithudi ine ndili kuopa kuti adzandikana.”
“Ndipondikhozakupsamtimandikulepherakuyankhula. Tumizani Aroni.”
“Ndipo iwo ali ndi mangawa ndi ine ndipo ndichita mantha kuti akhoza kukandipha.”
Mulungu adati, “Nkosatheka kutero! Kotero pitani nonse awiri ndi zizindikiro zathu. Ife tidzakhala ndi inu ndipo tidzamva.”
Ndipo mukakafika kwa Farawo mukamuuze kuti, “Ife ndife Atumwi ochokera kwa Ambuye wa zolengedwa zonse.”
“Motero alekeni ana a Israyeli kuti apite ndi ife.”
(Farawo) adati, “Kodi ife sitidakurere iwe pamene udali wamng’ono? Ndipo iwe unakhala pakati pathu zaka zambiri.”
“Ndipo iwe udachita chimene udachita. Ndithudi iwe ndiwe mmodzi wa anthu osathokoza.”
(Mose) adati, “Ine ndidachita chimenecho popeza nthawi imeneyo ndidali wosadziwa china chilichonse.”
“Motero ine ndidathawa inu nonse pa nthawi imene ndidakuopani koma tsopano Ambuye wanga wandipatsa luntha ndiponso wandipanga ine kukhala mmodzi mwa Atumwi ake.”
“Ndipo uwu ndi mwayi umene ubwino wake iwe uli kundinyogodola. Iwe wasandutsa ana a Israyeli kukhala akapolo ako.”
Farawo adati, “Kodi Ambuye wa zolengedwa zonse ndani?”
(Mose) adati, “Ambuye wa kumwamba ndi dziko lapansi ndi zonse zimene zili pakati pawo ngati inu mufuna kukhulupirira.”
(Farawo) adawafunsa anthu amene adamuzungulira! “Kodi muli kumva zimene ali kunenazi.”
(Mose) adapitiriza kuti, “Ambuye wanu ndiponso Ambuye wa makolo anu akale.”
(Farawo) adati, “Ndithudi Mtumwi amene watumizidwa kwa inu ndi wopenga.”
(Mose) adati, “Iye ndi Ambuye wa kum’mawa ndi kumadzulo ndi zonse zimene zikhala kumeneko ngati muli ozindikira.”
(Farawo) adayankha kuti, “Ngati iwe utumikira mulungu wina kupatula ine, ndithudi ndikupanga kukhala mmodzi wa anthu okhala ku ndende.”
(Mose) adafunsa kuti, “Kodi zingakhale choncho ngakhale nditakulangiza chizindikiro choonekeratu? “
(Farawo) adati, “Tilangize chizindikiro chako ngati zonse zimene unena ndi zoona.”
Motero Mose adaponya ndodo yake pansi ndipo nthawi yomweyo idasanduka njoka yeniyeni
Ndipo Iye adatulutsa dzanja lake ndipo nthawi yomweyo lidasanduka loyera kwa iwo amene adaliona
Farawo adauza nduna zake kuti, “Ndithudi munthu uyu ndi wodziwa matsenga.”
“Iyeyu afuna kukuchotsani m’dziko lanu ndi matsenga ake. Kodi ulangizi wanu ndi wotani ndipo ukupereka langizo lanji?”
Iwo adati, “Muyambe mwawasunga iye pamodzi ndi m’bale wake kwa kanthawi kochepa. Tumizani mithenga ku mizinda yanu
Abweretse kwa inu munthu aliyense yemwe ndi wodziwa matsenga kwambiri.”
Motero anthu amatsengawa adasonkhanitsidwa patsiku lodziwika lomwe adagwirizana
Ndipo anthu adafunsidwa kuti, “Kodi nonse mudzasonkhana?”
“Kuti mwina ife tikhoza kudzatsatira a matsenga ngati iwo atapambana.”
Ndipo pamene anthu onse amatsenga adadza kwa Farawo, iwo adati kwa Farawo, “Kodi mudzatilipira ngati titapambana?”
Iye adati, “Inde. Ndipo ndithudi inu mudzakhala kufupi ndi Ine.”
Mose adawauza kuti, “Ponyani pansi chilichonse chimene mufuna kuponya.”
Ndipo iwo adaponya zingwe ndi ndodo zawo ndipo adati: “Mwa mphamvu ya Farawo, ndithudi, ife tipambana.”
Ndipo Mose adaponya ndodo yake ndipo nthawi yomweyo idameza zonse zabodza zimene iwo adapanga
Ndipo anthu amatsenga onse aja adagwa pansi mogwada
Iwo adati, “Ife takhulupirira mwa Ambuye wa zolengedwa zonse.”
“Ambuye wa Mose ndi Aroni”
Farawo adati, “Kodi inu mwakhulupirira mwa iye pamene ine sindinakupatseni chilolezo? Ndithudi iye ndi mtsogoleri wanu amene adakuphunzitsani matsenga. Ndithudi posachedwapa mudzazindikira. Ndithudi ine ndidzadula manja anu ndi miyendo yanu moisiyanitsa. Ndidzakudulani dzanja lamanja ndi mwendo wamanzere ndiponso ndidzakupachikani pa mtanda.”
Iwo adati, “Zilibe kanthu chifukwa ndithudi ife tidzabwerera kwa Ambuye wathu.”
“Ndithudi Ife tili ndi chiyembekezo kuti Ambuye wathu adzatikhululukira machimo athu popeza ndife oyamba kukhulupirira.”
Ndipo tidamulamula Mose kuti, “Nyamuka nthawi ya usiku ndi akapolo anga chifukwa, ndithudi, inu mulondoledwa ndi gulu la adani anu.”
Ndipo Farawo adatumiza mithenga ku mizinda yonse
“Ndithudi anthu amenewa ndi kagulu ka anthu ochepa.”
“Ndithudi anthu amenewa atipsetsa mtima.”
“Ife tonse tili tcheru.”
Ndipo tidawachotsa m’minda ndi mu a kasupe
Ndiponso m’chuma ndi m’malo alionse olemekezeka
Kotero tidawapanga ana a Israyeli kukhala alowa m’malo a zinthu za anthu a Farawo
Pamene dzuwa linali kutuluka, iwo adalondoledwa ndi adani awo
Ndipo pamene magulu awiriwa adaonana wina ndi mnzake, anthu a Mose adati, “Ndithudi atipeza.”
Mose adati, “Iyayi. Ndithudi Ambuye wanga ali ndi ine ndipo adzanditsogolera.”
Ndipo tidalamulira Mose kuti, “Menya madzi a m’nyanja ndi ndodo yako.” Ndipo nyanja idagawanika pakati, mbali iliyonse idali ngati phiri lalikulu
Ndipo anthu a Farawo tidawayandikitsa ndi nyanja ija
Ndipo Ife tidapulumutsa Mose ndi onse amene adali ndi iye
Ndipo tidamiza ena
Ndithudi mu ichi muli phunziro komabe anthu ambiri sakhulupirira ayi
Ndithudi Ambuye wako! Iye ndiye Mwini mphamvu zonse ndi Mwini chisoni chosatha
Ndipo afotokozere nkhani za Abrahamu
Pamenepo iye adanena kwa abambo ake ndiponso kwa anthu ake kuti, “Kodi ndi chiyani chimene inu muli kupembedza?”
Iwo adati, “Timatumikira mafano ndipo timapempha kwa iwo modzipereka kwambiri.”
Ndipo adati, “Kodi iwo amakumvani pamene mumawapempha?”
“Kodi amakuthandizani kapena kukuonongani?”
Iwo adati, “Iyayi. Koma ife tidawapeza makolo athu akupembedza mafano.”
Iye adati, “Kodi inu muli kuzidziwa zimene muli kuzipembedza?”
“Inu ndiponso makolo anu akale?”
“Ndithudi onse ndi adani anga kupatula Ambuye wachilengedwe.”
“Amene adandipanga ine ndipo ndiye amene amandipatsa chilangizo.”
“Ndipo ndiye amene amandipatsa chakudya ndi chakumwa.”
“Ndipo ndikadwala, ndi Iye amene amandichiza.”
“Ndipo ndiye amene adzandipangitsa kuti ndife ndi kudzandibwezeranso moyo.”
“Ndi amene ine ndimayembekezera kuti adzandikhululukira machimo anga pa tsiku lachiweruzo”
Ambuye ndipatseni luntha ndipo mundilole kuti ndikhale pakati pa anthu ochita zabwino
Ndipatseni ulemerero umene udzatchulidwe ndi mibadwo yomwe ikubwera mtsogolo
Ndipo ndiikeni m’gulu la anthu amene adzakhala kumalo a mtendere a ku Paradiso
Akhululukireni abambo anga ndithudi iwo ali mmodzi mwa anthu osochera
Musadzandichititse manyazi patsiku limene anthu adzaukitsidwa kwa akufa
Tsiku limene chuma ndi ana sizidzathandiza wina aliyense
Kupatula yekhayo amene adzadza kwa Mulungu ndi mtima woyera
Pamenepo Paradiso idzayandikiritsidwa kwa anthu angwiro
Ndipo Gahena idzaonetsedwa poyera kwa anthu ochimwa
Mawu adzanenedwa kwa iwo kuti, “Kodi mafano anu aja amene mumatumikira ali kuti?”
Kuwonjezera pa Mulungu weniweni? Kodi iwo akhoza kukuthandizani inu kapena kudzithandiza okha?”
Ndipo iwo ndi onse ochimwa adzaponyedwa ku Gahena
Ndiponso pamodzi ndi magulu onse a Satana
Iwo adzati pamene adzakhala ali kukangana kumeneko
“Pali Mulungu, ndithudi, ife tidali ochimwa moonekeratu.”
Pamene tidakusandutsani inu kukhala ofanana ndi Ambuye wa zolengedwa zonse
Palibe ena koma anthu ochita zoipa amene adatisocheretsa ife
Palibe wina woti angatipepesere ife
Ndiponso palibe bwenzi lenileni
Koma tikadakhalanso ndi moyo, tikadakhala anthu okhulupirira
Ndithudi mu zimenezi muli chizindikiro koma anthu ambiri sakhulupirira ayi
Ndithudi Ambuye wanu! Ndiye Mwini mphamvu zonse ndi Mwini chisoni chosatha
Anthu a m’badwo wa Nowa adakana Atumwi awo
Pamene Nowa adati, “Kodi inu simungaope Mulungu ndi kumumvera Iye?”
“Ndithudi ine ndine Mtumwi wanu wokhulupirika.”
“Motero opani Mulungu ndipo mundimvere ine.”
“Ine sindikupemphani malipiro ena alionse chifukwa palibe wina aliyense amene angandilipire ine kupatula Ambuye wa zolengedwa zonse.”
“Kotero opani Mulungu ndipo mundimvere ine.”
Iwo adati, “Kodi ife tikukhulupirire iwe pamene anthu onyozeka ndiwo amene amakutsatira iwe?”
Nowa adati, “Kodi ine ndikudziwa chiyani za chimene iwo amachita?”
“Ambuye wanga ndiye amene akhoza kuweruza ngati mumazindikira.”
“Ndipo ine sindidzathamangitsa anthu okhulupirira moona.”
“Ine ndine wopereka chenjezo poyera.”
Iwo adati, “Iwe Nowa; ngati siusiya zimene uchita udzaponyedwa miyala.”
Iye adati, “Ambuye wanga! Ndithudi anthu anga akundikana.”
Motero weruzani mwachilungamo pakati pa ine ndi iwo. Ndipulumutseni ine pamodzi ndi anthu okhulupirira amene ali ndi ine
Ife tidamupulumutsa iye pamodzi ndi iwo amene adali naye m’chombo
Ndipo pambuyo pake tidamiza ena onse ndi chigumula
Ndithudi mu chimenechi muli phunziro komabe ambiri sakhulupirira
Ndithudi Ambuye wako ndi Mwini mphamvu ndi Mwini chisoni chosatha
Anthu a ku Aad sanakhulupirire Atumwi awo
Pamene m’bale wawo Houd adati, “Kodi inu simungakhale ndi mantha ndi Mulungu?”
“Ndithudi ine ndine Mtumwi wanu wokhulupirika.”
“opani Mulungu ndipo munditsate ine.”
“Pa ntchito iyi, ine sindipempha malipiro kuchokera kwa inu chifukwa palibe wina amene angandilipire kupatula Ambuye wa zolengedwa zonse.”
“Kodi inu mukumamanga nyumba pamalo paliponse pokwera mofuna kudzisangalatsa?”
“Kodi muli kumanga nyumba zokongola ndi zolimba ngati kuti mudzakhalamo mpaka kalekale?”
“Ndipo pamene mumenya anthu mumamenya ngati anthu ankhanza.”
“Motero opani Mulungu, ndipo mundimvere ine.”
“Ndipo muopeni Iye amene wakupatsani inu zinthu zonse zimene mumazidziwa.”
“Iye wakupatsani nyama ndi ana,”
“Ndiponso minda ndi a kasupe;”
“Ndithudi ine ndili kuchita mantha ndi chilango chimene chidzadza pa inu pa tsiku loopsa.”
Iwo adati, “Ndi chimodzimodzi kwa ife kaya utilalikira kapena ayi.”
“Zonse zimene uli kutiopseza nazo ndi chikhalidwe cha anthu amakedzana.”
